 aṃśam nidadhati svam svam karma bhoga prasiddhaye aka ātma parijñānāt dhvasta avidyasya sarvatas  akāraka ātmanā tasthau pratyak dṛṣṭiḥ asaṃgataḥ akārakā dvaya tvābhyām draṣṭu tvam na akṣara ātmanaḥ akārya kāraṇam sākṣāt ityādi guṇa lakṣaṇam akārya kāraṇa ātmā etad vāstavam rūpam ātmanaḥ akatsna daṣṭi viṣayaḥ  niṣedhaḥ api na yajyate akrata tvām yatas  viprāḥ saṃdaṃśam mayi pāvake akṣaram yadi na sthalamaṇa tarhi tad iṣyatām akṣaram yena rūpeṇa sthalam vastu niṣedhati akṣaram yaḥ  viditvā asmāt lokāt nārgi pramīyate akṣaram sva ātma saṃmohāt kāraṇa tvam nigacchati akṣarasya śrutiḥ sākṣāt tad vā iti evamādinā akṣara ajñānataḥ paṃsān kārpaṇyena aviyakta tāma akṣara ātmani na astitve tasmāt hetak tiḥ iṣyate akṣara ātmā avasānānām parva parva prahāṇataḥ akṣara anteṣu tattveṣu na avyākṛta vacaḥ  yatas  akṣare tad asaṃbhāvyam amātram tad yatas tatas  akṣīṇaiḥ karma saṃtānaiḥ tathā eva janayati api agṛhyamāṇam sat tattvam viparītam iva īkṣyate agauṇa avyavadhāna ādi viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tā agniḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ  vā hi āpaḥ tad kāraṇam matāḥ agnihotra agni saṃskāram yatas  na avāpa śāpataḥ agnīṣoma ātmanā śrutyā dhyāna artham iha bhaṇyate agni ādayaḥ tathā lokā amṛta ādyāḥ ca devatāḥ agni ādi dṛṣṭibhiḥ ca asya dehaḥ prāc pratipāditaḥ agni ādi devatā aṃśā ye bhoga artham karmaṇā arjitāḥ agni ādi devatāḥ saḥ ayam apasaṃhāra ucyate agni ādi devatānām ca vyāptiḥ etāvatī matā agni ādiṣa yatas  ṣaṭsa yathā uktāḥ sarva devatāḥ aṅgam vā vīryavat daṣṭam paṃsān prāyeṇa dakṣiṇam aṅgāra aṅkitamad pāte vāri rāśeḥ iva udakam aṅgārāva kṣayaṇa uktyā vidvān ki brahma śreyasaḥ acitka tvāt pradhāna ādi paṃsaḥ na sthānam iṣyate acintyā ca apratā ca prāṇa bhāvena ca sthitā acetanatva anityatva doṣa daṣṭam para uditam ajñāta jñātatas anyatva anirdeśyam na tad akṣaram ajñātasya prameyasya yuktaḥ sva dhvānta sākṣiṇaḥ ajñāna kāma janya tvam vāc manaḥ kāya karmaṇām ajñāna dhvaṃsa kāri tvāt mokṣaḥ  jñānasya bhaṇyate ajñāna bhami gam vastu māna saṃgatim āpnavat  ajñānam anabhivyaktiḥ bodhaḥ abhivyaktiḥ ātmanaḥ ajñānam anirākarvat jñānam eva na sidhyati ajñānam āgama jñānam sāṃgatyam na asti atas anayoḥ ajñāna mātra vyavadhau vastani vyāpatiḥ miteḥ ajñāna hānam naḥ muktiḥ tasyāḥ karma na sādhanam ajñāna ādi trayam pratyagābhāsam yadi api iṣyate ajñāna anya artha vijñāna prasaktau  eva yajyate ajñāna ani āvijñāna prasaṅga aṅgīkṛtau  api aṇu mātram na tad grāhya vastu yaniṣpramāṇakam aṇan pratyekaśaḥ sarvān sa gṛhṇīyāt ayatnataḥ aṇḍasya antaḥ tu ime lokāḥ sapta dvīpā ca medinī aṇḍābahis  purāṇe tu virodhe smṛti bādhanam aṇḍa antam eva vyākhyātam kim anyat avaśiṣyate aṇḍa ārambhaka bhatānām brahma loka abhidhā iṣyate aṇu antān iti śabdaḥ ayam na syāt paśu viśeṣaṇam atas  kāma āśaya vaśāt sṛjyate annam muhur muhur  atas  param prayatnena śrutyā vyākhyāyate sphuṭam atad vabodha eva etad sidhyati iva na ta svatas  atas tad tvam asīti aktyā tādātmyam pratipādyate atādātmyāt na hi ghaṭam janayanti iha tantavaḥ ati nirbandhataḥ  vā api niṣedhyaḥ ayam pramādavān ati nirmathanāt agniḥ candanāt api jāyate ati pramāṇa viṣayam brahma sarvatra viśrutam ati mokṣāḥ syaḥ sarvatra yathā uktāt eva lakṣaṇāta atimokṣa atideśa ukteḥ tad viśeṣaḥ atha bhaṇyate ati sakṣmābhiḥ etābhiḥ jagdham annam samāsravata atīta anāgatayoḥ ta kālayoḥ jagadātmanaḥ atītya vasta vṛttena sva mahimna vyavasthitaḥ atas akṣaram pravaktavyam nirupādhya ātmani sthitam atas avagatiḥ eva atra gati tvena vivakṣyate atas avagati abhāvaḥ api na svatas avagatim vinā atas  jitā hṛtā gāvaḥ  yātāḥ sarve yathāyatham atas  brāhmaṇī atas anyat yad kriyā kāraka lakṣaṇam atas  yathā uktāt etasmāt sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇāta atyavādīḥ tvam ajñaḥ sankā vidyā phalinī tava atyeti vasta vṛttena sa sākṣāt iti gṛhyatāma atyeti iti tu ye pāṭham kurvate te avipaścitaḥ atra yad prativaktavyam tad aktamasakṛt parā atha kaḥ saṃśayaḥ  yena sa tena evam niyajyate atha brāhmaṇa iti aktyā phala avasthā asya bhaṇyate athavā lakṣaṇa uktiḥ syāt yathā ukta brahma vedinaḥ atha saṃbhaya savīṇi mokta kamoṇi kavete atha eṣa eva iti ca tathā udarke pravakṣyate atha eṣa eva paramaḥ  yaḥ  vai bhameti śāstrataḥ atha upacārataḥ  mokṣaḥ kāryam syāt nityakarmaṇaḥ adāhakaḥ api vahniḥ sandāhya dravya samāśrayāt adīrgham iti atas  dravyam na syāt akṣaram avyayam adṛṣṭa phala saṃprepsoīṣṭa karma phalatyajaḥ adaṣṭaḥ aśrata iti aktyā kriyate jñāna śaddhaye adbhiḥ antar bahis ca iyam vyāptā eva iha samīkṣyate adbhiḥ ca iyam kṣitiāptā tasmāt tāsām api iṣyate advitīya padārthasya tathā na eva ātmanaḥ anyatas  advitīya artha niṣṭha tvam ātma pratyaya śabdayoḥ advaita darśana arthāya śāstra ārambhaḥ ata eva ca advaita darśanena atas  na asti kiṃcid prayojanam advaita darśanena asya dvaitat aṣṭi apanattaye advaitān abhisaṃbandhaḥ  na āśaḥ vā malaśat dhivata adhikāra viśeṣeṇa pṛthivī ityādinā adhunā adhikāri viśeṣasya jñānāya brāhmaṇa grahaḥ adhidaivam ca vibhvīyam dvaita eka tvena viṣṭhitā adhidaiva ātmanā teṣām dṛṣṭayaḥ sādhana ātma nām adhidaiva ātmanā vetti sa hotā evaṃvidhaḥ  bhaveta adhibhatam tathā asya eva vāya mayyaḥ samantagāḥ adhibhūta ātmanā eva ayam nāḍī lakṣaṇa vartmanā adhibhatā adhiyajña ādi pariccheda phala ātmakaḥ adhiṣṭhātṛ viyaktāni nyasta dātra upamāni hi adhyasta diniṣedhaḥ ca vyomni ekasmin yathā tathā adhyasya ātmani deha ādīn maḍhaḥ tadvat viceṣṭate adhyātmam cakṣuḥ adhvaryuḥ adhi yajñam dvayam raviḥ adhyātma prāṇa eva syāt agātā yaḥ adhiyajña gaḥ adhyātma devatāḥ sarvā hṛdi nītvā ātmanaḥ tatas  adhyātma ādi paricchedāt i athā ukta upāsana āśrayāta adhyātma ādi vyavacchedāt macyamāna upāsanaiḥ adhyātma ādiṣa kātsyena teṣa teṣu avatiṣṭhate adhyātma ādi adhiyajña ādeḥ ādhidaivata rūpa tā adhvaryuḥ aham eva iti sākṣātkṛtvā vimucyate ananuśiṣṭa hetu uktyā matī rājñaḥ tadā bhavat ananta bhinna kāryeṣu samāptiḥ devatā ātmanaḥ ananta bheda bhinnasya punar api aṣṭadhā ucyate anantam eva tena asau samyak jñānena vindati anantaram aparvasya kārya nirdiśyate adhanā ananta vigrahaḥ saḥ agniḥ hotā mṛtyoḥ yathā uditāt ananyamama ṣaṣṭhī artham vaiśabdaḥ tad prasiddhaye ananya hetukam tāvat  trayam etad yathā uditam ananya anubhava ātma ābham tad pramāṇam sadādaśeḥ ananya apekṣa saṃsiddheḥ deśa ādeḥ tad apekṣataḥ anara uktau tu tātparya yukteḥ arthaḥ  na yuktitaḥ anātmatva prasaktiḥ syāt raṣṭa dṛśya prabhedataḥ anātmatva prasiddhiḥ syāt liṅga piṇḍa ātmanā urataḥ anātma tvam atas  siddham prāṇa ādeḥ karaṇa uktitaḥ anātma māna mayaḥ arthaḥ  yatas atas  kevala ātma tā anātma artha niṣedhena yaḥ  na iti iti purā uditaḥ anātyantika rūpa tvāt atyayaḥ asau na gṛhyate anārabhyatva vacanam tad hetu pratipattaye anārabhyā tu iyam muktiḥ tad siddharjñāna hetutaḥ anārambhaḥ ca śanye api yathā ayam apalabhyate anirmātā ātmayā athātmyaiḥ yad tu kaiścid iha ucyate anirmokṣa prasaktiḥ syāt tasya ca āsaṅga rūpataḥ anirmokṣa prasaktiḥ ca kṣetrajña paramātmanoḥ anivṛtte satī bhayaḥ avidyām janayitam kṣame aniṣṭhitam na karma api phalāya alam bhavet  kvacid  anamāna śratiḥ tasmāt āgāt tasya eva siddhaye anuśiṣyā api sa nṛpam yadā na aicchat dhanam nṛpāt  anusaṃdheyam atra api vastu tattva viśuddhaye anadya apeta duḥkhena sākṣāt saṃgatim abravīt anadya eva yathāprāptam ātma dṛṣṭiḥ vidhīyate anena vidhṛtam janma vāyunā idam śarīrakam antaḥkaraṇa vṛttiḥ yā cakṣuḥ ādi samāśrayā antar  saṃsthāpya nayati samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi tāmasaḥ antarikṣam anādhāram gatau heta niṣedha nama antaraḥ  yaḥ pṛthivyāḥ syāt kṣiteḥ abhyantaraḥ  hi yaḥ antaryāmi iti saḥ atra api na atas anyaḥ asti iti bhaṇyate antaryāmī paraḥ sākṣāt aśarīraḥ agaṇaḥ advayaḥ antaryāmya ādi rūpeṇa sa eva prathate mṛṣā andhakāraḥ tamaḥ  jñeyam tathā chāyā mayaḥ pumān annam dāma iti yad pūrvam vyākhyātam śiśu bandhanam annam nāḍī āśrayam sakṣma tad śutya iha upavarṇyate annam prāṇaḥ ca devau dvau dvayoḥ eṣa vinirṇayaḥ annasya praviveka artham bhoktaḥ saukṣmya artham eva ca anna aśitṛtva siddhayartham yathā vyutpattiḥ ucyate annena aśnuta iti evam adhyardhasya api yojanā anyathākṛtsnam eva syāt anirmokṣaḥ ca sajyate anyathā anupapattyā ced viśva jitvat prakalpyate anyathā api upapanna tvāt āpatteḥ kṣayaḥ  yatas  anyat hi mukti phalataḥ kāmyānām śrūyate phalam anya yoga vyavacchede praśaṃseyam asoḥ bhavet  anya anapekṣam sat mānam prameya artha samarpakam anyāsādhāraṇam praśnam aprākṣīt iti vismitaḥ anye atas  mṛtyavaḥ  gauṇāḥ taiḥ mṛtau syāt punaniḥ anye amṛtam idam prāhar divyam cāndramasam payaḥ anye gati vivakṣa artham maneḥ praśnam pracakṣate anyena kenacid vyāptiāpaka tvāt yathā bhavaḥ anyena anyena rūpeṇa viruddhān hanti pāvakaḥ anvakṣam eva vilayaḥ  dṛśyate sārvalaukikaiḥ apanyāyaḥ  na yuktaḥ atas  nyāya vasim anvayāt aparicchinna saṃvyāpti jya praśnena bhaṇyate apare paṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ samyak jñāta ātma tattvakāḥ aparokṣāt bhavet tādṛś nātaḥ anyādṛś katham cana aparokṣa antam athavā brahma antam vā uttarasya tu apavādasya viṣayaḥ  jñāta ātmā eka sa tattvakaḥ apām guṇaḥ atra snehaḥ syāt chāyā dīptiḥ iha iṣyate apānena āhṛtaḥ  gandhaḥ  ghrāṇasya eti vaśam yathā apām annam bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ  bahvīnām tanu vigrahaḥ apāsta aśeṣa nirdeśam yad ananya pramāṇakam apāsta aśeṣa an artha āpta paruṣa artha tvataḥ svatas  api khe tad asaṃbhāvyam kim tad pratyagātmani api ced vakti anirdeśyam kathaṃcid moha vibhramāt  api dṛṣṭa kriyā dharma sāmarthyam anirasya tu api dhānāruhaḥ  vṛkṣaḥ  bījāt tad janma darśanāta api prāptam karma kāṇḍe tad virodhāt ta na abravīt  api śāstra artha saṃbandha uttarasyāḥ śruteḥ ayam api samyak pramāṇaśāḥ tad ca na ṛte maheśvaram apam artham idam prāptam na ced ātmā eva tad bhaveta aparvam niṣpramāṇam ca dātam śaktiḥ atha asya ca aparva ādiṣa jīvatsa śruti vākyeṣa śakyate aparva ādi ātmakam brahma niḥsaṃsargam prapadyate aparvān aparāyekaḥ parṇaḥ sva ātmani avasthitaḥ aparvān apara ananta tattvam brahmā eva vākyataḥ apekṣā vṛttavat vasta yāvat kicid iha īkṣyate api ajñāta ātma yāthātmyaḥ  jijñāsuḥ yaḥ atra vastuni api advayam param brahma dvayavat prathate mṛṣā api abhāvaḥ  na labhate kim u bhāvaḥ atireka tām aprameyam hi yad vasta na tad śakyam pramāṇataḥ apraviśya prayogam tad vittam iti apadiśyate aprasiddha abhidhāna uktyā vādivyāmoha siddhaye aprākṣīt paramātmānam kaholaḥ api na dākhinam aprāpta tattva niṣṭhaḥ atas  pāṇḍitye viniyajyate ap da īśā pṛthivī kṛtsnā tejaḥ deśam tathā jalama abravīt abhrānti mātra tvam mṛttikā ādi nidarśanaiḥ abrahma anātma apahanati ā saṃsarga kātmyadhīḥ bhavet abrahmiṣṭhatva siddhayartham atas aprākṣī draṣa anvitaḥ abhayam tvām iti katham rājñā āśīḥ tam pratīryate abhayam tvām iti nṛpaḥ  yathā ukta jñāna liṅganam abhayam tvām iti prāha yājñavalkyam sa pārthivaḥ abhayam tvām iti vacaḥ tad hayasya aprāptam acyate abhayam vedayasi iti etad na ca asākṣātkṛte pare abhayasya pradātṛtva ananvavāpta abhayaḥ guruḥ abhāvatva niṣedha artham draṣṭrakṣaram iha ucyate abhāvasya api tad sākṣyāt tad abhāvaḥ katas  miteḥ abhāvāt ca tvad anyasya sarvam ātmā iti śāsanāt  abhinna mātṛ mān ādiḥ ātmā eva ekaḥ advayaḥ svatas  abhivyaktam ca sat idam punar avyakta tāmitam abhivyaṅgayasa jātīyaḥ  vyañjakaḥ  rūpa dīpavat  abhyantaratamam sūtram brahma loka avadheḥ api amama aparigraha uktaiḥ niṣkarmā muniḥ ucyate amṛtiḥ ca api anutkrāntau satsu prāṇeṣu kā mṛtiḥ ayathāvastu avidyā syāt vidyetasyā virodhinī artha antara tvāt yaktīnām pramāṇebhyaḥ  yatas tatas  arthāpatti kṣayaḥ atas  syāt anyathā api apapattitaḥ arthāpatteḥ aparvasya kalpanā api na yajyate arthāpatteḥ ca tatra eva kṣīṇa tvāt mokṣa kalpane ardha tvam syāt kanīyaḥ tu ādvaya api asya agni ādi rūpiṇaḥ arvāk eva akṣarāt jñeyā satteyam jagataḥ  nidhiḥ arvāk yad ca kapālāt syāt madhye yad ca kapālayoḥ avatiṣṭhata eva ayam kim vā karma eva saṃśritaḥ avaśiṣṭam ca yad tad ca na pramāṇa upapāditam avaśiṣṭam yad api asya tad mām pṛcchatu kāmataḥ avaśyam ced prakalpyam syāt puṃspravṛtti prayojakam avāpta aśeṣa kāme asau bhavan  tad mohataḥ  bhavet  avicārita saṃsiddha pratyagajñāna lakṣaṇam avicārita saṃsiddhitamaḥvat syāt tad bhavam avicārita saṃsiddhi pratyagajñāna saṃsthitiḥ avicārita saṃsiddhi moha upahata cetasāma avidyān anvayādāsvat pratyagjyotiḥ sa tattvataḥ avidyā nāśa mātraḥ ca mokṣa ātmana iṣyate avidyā mātra vidhvastau yatas anāptavat āpyate avidyā mātra vyavadhiḥ yatas  mokṣaḥ abhyapeyate avidyā eka udbhava tvam syāt yadi api jñāna karmaṇoḥ avinirbhāga vṛtti tvāt sarvadā eva parasparam avyākṛta girā tasya vyākṛta avyākṛta tvataḥ avyākṛta vyākaraṇe yad uktam sarvam eva tad  avyākṛta ādi bhāvena vrīhi ādi tvāya janyate avyāvṛttān anugatam astu brahma iti bhaṇyate avyāvṛtta ānana gatam caitanyam saṃvid īkṣyatām avyāvṛttān anugatam tatas api akṣara saṃjñitam avyāvṛttān anugatam brahmāgauṇam pracakṣate avyāvṛtta ānana gatam brahma ātmā eva tatas  bhavet  avyāvṛttān anugataḥ pūrṇaḥ sva ātmani avasthitaḥ avyāvṛtta ānana gata bhāsvat vijñāna mātrataḥ aśaknavan  tathā karta liṅgena pratibodhayeta aśanāya ādikān  tasmāt kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇān aśanāya ādi nirmaktam sākṣāt ityādi lakṣaṇam aśanāya ādi saṃbandhaḥ samyak bodhādataḥ hanatiḥ aśanāya ādi saṃbandhaḥ  na ātmanaḥ  vāstavaḥ  mataḥ aśanāya ādi atikrānta dṛṣṭi draṣṭu padārthayoḥ aśanāya ādi atikrāntyā praśna artha āviṣkṛtiḥ kṛtā aśanāya ādi atīta tvam parva uktasya eva vastanaḥ aśanāyā pi pāsā ādi dharmiṇam prāhuḥ īśvaram aśanāyā pipāsābhyām tasmāt tad kāraṇa grahaḥ aśanāyā pipāse dve eva na atyeti kevale aśanāyā pipāse yaḥ tad hetoḥ atyayāt sadā aśeṣa viṣaya ātma tvam manaḥ buddhayoḥ vinirdiśet  aśvamedha kṛtaḥ  yatra parve tastharitaḥ  gatāḥ aśvamedha kṛtaḥ  vakti bhajyuḥ pārikṣitā iti aśvamedha kratoḥ eṣa samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi lakṣaṇaḥ aśvamedha makhā parvam devatā agniḥ iha ucyate aśvamedha makhā parva phala prakathanena yā aśvalaḥ api aparame atha sva ukta praśna vinirṇayāta aṣṭadhātar  punar tasya bhedaḥ ayam upavarṇyate aṣṭau  āyatanāni atra pṛthivī ādīni nirdiśet  asaṃvedyam sukham mokṣe kecid na iti pracakṣate asaṃtoṣāt kaholaḥ ata uṣasta praśnam eva tu asamastam idam brahma na yuktam samupāsitum asamāpteḥ pum arthasya matam na asya anuśāsanam asamāsena nirdeśaḥ  bhinna kāryatva kāraṇāta asaṃbhavāt tad anyatra brahma tvasya yatas tatas  asaṃbhavaḥ  yathā mukteḥ kriyā sādhana saṃśrayāt  asākṣikam ced chanya tvam sākṣi vatsyāt asākṣikam asādhanatvāt na api āpyaḥ pratyak mātra svabhāvataḥ asādhāraṇa dharma uttham vijñānam vastani pramā asādha araṇya siddhayartham āvām ā iva iti atas avadat  asti ced anavasthā syāt anirmokṣaḥ  na ced bhavet  asti tāvat ayam lokaḥ  yathā ukta parimāṇavān astitvam akṣarasya iha siddham tāvat ga ātmanaḥ astitva vyatirikta tve baddhasya ca viniścite astitve tasya saṃsiddhe tad muktyai yatyate yatas  asti na asti iti vā brahi yājñavalkya yathātatham asti mānam yatas  nityam karma sarvatra codyate astu kāmam tad udgātuḥ na tu tad yajamāna gam astu saṅga ātmakam tarhi vāsanā saṅga darśanāta asthūla tvāt na tad śakyam nirdeṣṭum iti saḥ abravīt  asthūlaḥ anaṇuḥ iti evam akṣara ātma avadhāritaḥ astha lokti samuttha ātma yāthātmya jñāna vahninā asthaulyāt aṇa tad prāptam tad nānaṇa yatas akṣaram asmad anyatra manvīthā yatra idam hṛdayam kvacita asmin praśāstari sati kriyā tad phala saṃgateḥ asya pratyak padārthasya hi ā samāpteḥ vidhīyate aham mama iti avidyādhīḥ sa hetuḥ nāśitā yadā ahaṃrūpeṇa yaḥ anveti sa pramātā paraḥ  mataḥ ahaṃdṛṣṭi adhigamya tvam api draṣṭuḥ iha iṣyate aham asmi pṛthivī ekā bibharmi jagat avyayam ahallikā iti vacasā na ādhāra antaram ucyate ahorātre tatas  mṛtyuḥ tābhyām muktiḥ kutaḥ bhavet  ākāraḥ  jāyate anityaḥ  duḥkha śabda ādi lakṣaṇaḥ ākāraḥ  jāyate baddheḥ āgama apāya dharmavānḥ ākāśa eva kim vā syāt iti evam pūrva śeṣa tā ākāśa vacasā ātmā eva jñeyaḥ  na anyaḥ atra kaśa cana ākāśaḥ tasya sarvasya tattvam atra vivakṣitam ākāśe tad avijñātam sattā mātreṇa vidyate ākāśaḥ  vā iti tathā brahmā eva śrutiḥ abravīt  āgate na tu avidyāyāḥ  bhavatā eva etad acyate āgamasya pravṛttiḥ ta meya vṛtta vyapekṣayā āgama anautamaḥ aprākṣīt yājñavalkya madāra dhīḥ āgama artha viśuddhayartham yuktīḥ atra pravakṣyati āgama arthe yathā evam syāt yukti arthe na āgama īkṣaṇam āgama eka pradhāna tvam katham tasya iti bhaṇyate āgama eka pramāṇa tve vadanti iti abhiśabdanam āgama ukti pradhāna tvam madhuka aṇḍasya varṇitam ācchādikātaḥ sā yuktā samasta vyasta rūpiṇaḥ ātma jñāna udayāya eva yājñavalkyaḥ api atas avadat  ātma tvāt āpta tattvaḥ ayam na deśa ādi antarāyavān ātma dṛṣṭiḥ tu iyam nityā janma nāśa ādi varjitā ātma dṛṣṭyā tathā īkṣyante nānā ātmānaḥ  virodhataḥ ātma dhī viṣayam na eti tad ajñāna eka kāraṇaḥ ātmanaḥ tattva vijñānam tadvat na aṅgam kriyā vidhau ātmani iti śruteḥ vākyam apramāṇam prasajyate ātmanaḥ anavaśeṣeṇa tad anya arthasya saṃgataḥ ātmanaḥ anyat yatas  sarvam pañcabhata ātmakam vidaḥ ātmanaḥ api parokṣa tvam brahmaṇaḥ api tamaḥ nvayāt  ātmanaḥ  brahmatā iha uktā na tu anātmana īritā ātma pratyaya eka arthaḥ tathā śrati vacāṃsi api ātma pramātṛ mān ādeḥ anekasya iha saṃbhavāt  ātma mātra eka yāthātmyāt na muktau syāgatiḥ tatas  ātmayājī iti manunā sa eva iha abhidhīyate ātma saṃskṛtaye karma yaḥ karoti yathāvidhi ātmā atyeti iti saṃbandhaḥ  yaḥ aśanāya ādi lakṣaṇāna ātmānam veda bhoktāram veda sarvam jagat tathā ātmānam sa muniḥ pṛṣṭaḥ  yatas tam paryapṛcchata ātmānam eva iti atra eva na bhayaḥ atra abhidhīyate ātma anātma artha saṃdṛṣṭyoḥ sphuṭam naḥ pratyapīpadat  ātmā api brahmaṇaḥ anyatra na eva saṃbhāvyate yatas  ātma avayava eva ayam saryaḥ cakṣuḥ mama aṃśamāna ātmā vā ara iti aktau na eva anā tma kṣaṇe vidhiḥ ātma asāmānya caitanya rūpa utthena ātma gam tamaḥ ātmā svatas tu bhāsvat cit mātraḥ parṇaḥ  nirañjanaḥ ātmā iti ca pramātṛ ādeḥ āgam āpāyasākṣī api ātmā eva ānanda yāthātmyam na atas  jñāna ādi sādhanam ātyantikī sama  chittiḥ syāt ced mohasya kāraṇe ādadānā yatas  yanti tena ādityā amī smṛtāḥ ādadānā yatas  yanti mānām sthiti kāraṇam ādadīta āpti siddhayartham gantavyasya tathā eva ca ādau  abhihitam sarvam bandhanam sa prayojakama āditya varṇa vacanāt asta tad rohita ātmakam āditya antargataḥ  devaḥ  vyākhyāta āyatana ādikaḥ ādi antavattva ātta duḥkham duḥkha saṃskāra jam tathā ādhudāttatva liṅgena hi abhidhānam vidagdhavat  ādhāra ādheyayoḥ aikyāt pṛthivī agni ādiṣa triṣa ādhyātmikam pariccheda mukta darśana vartmanā ādhyātmikasya sarvasya kāryasya karaṇasya ca ādhyātmikasya iva puṃsaḥ kṛtsnā adhyātma adhibhūtayoḥ ānantyam nitya tā eva asya nāsnaḥ na vyakti bharitā ānantyam baha śabdena devānām prābravīt maniḥ ānantyam brahma tā ca asya darghaṭā syāt tathā sati ānandam brahma vijñānam sākṣāt ityādi lakṣaṇam ānanda jñāna viṣayā kalpanā iyam vṛthā śramaḥ ānanda brahma vijñāna padārtha ekatva hetutaḥ aānandavat vāśaṅkayoktiḥ yaḥ aśanāya iti pūrvikā ānanda eka svabhāva tvāt na ātmanaḥ sukha kāmi tā ānanda eka svabhāvaḥ asya suṣupte adhyavasīyate ānandaḥ  brahma iti tathā taittirīya śrutau śrutam āpādya gamayāmāsa tatra prāṇa eka rūpiṇaḥ āparyedam jagat sarvam sthita ādhyātmikaḥ pumān āpta aśeṣa pamartha tvāt na apekṣā sādhanam prati ābrahma āsthāṇa ca ajasram yaḥ saṃsarati maḍha dhīḥ ābhavāt arjitānām ta sarveṣām api karmaṇā āma ābhāti bahudhā eva iyam tad avidyā uttha hetabhiḥ ābhāsa ādi pramāṇa antam tad viśiṣṭa phala utthiteḥ āyar vīryam smṛti prajñām saukam āryam vapuḥ śriyam ārabhyatva abhyupagame makteḥ tad syāt yathā uditam ārabhyamāṇa tā makteḥ pratyajñāyi tvayā eva sā ārabhye arthe aphalam jñānam vyañjaka tvāt pradīpavata ārambhaka tvam jagati tasyāḥ  na eva upapadyate ārambhaka baha tvāt ca bahuktiḥ iha gṛhyate ārurukṣoḥ maneḥ yogam karma kāraṇam acyate ārtam vināśi tad jñeyam brahmānārtam yatas tatas  ārtam vināśi tad tad cham śakti kāra jata ādivat  ārta bhāgaḥ  manirvidvān sa ca na iti tam abravīta āvayoḥ eva vijñānam yathā idam prāc abhaditaḥ āvām ā iva tathā eva ūrdhvam vediṣyā  aḥ  yathā uditam āviriñca āditas  bhapa yāsyasi kva iti bhaṇyatāma ā śākalyāt paraḥ  grantha itas  vyākhyāyate adhanā āśrayam kva iti paṃsaḥ asau  aprākṣīt mani sattamam āsaṅga eva bhatānām apādānam iha iṣyate āsaṅga kāryam acchinnam dvaitat aṣṭi ātmanaḥ  yatas  āsaṅgaḥ ca tathā eva āste te ete saṅga karmaṇī āsarāt karmaṇaḥ  mṛtyoratimaktiḥ iha uditā āsarāt sādhanāda eva prāptiḥ maktiḥ iha ucyate āsu eva upaniṣatsu enam yatas  vyācakṣate badhāḥ icchā tad sādhanānām ca syāt ānantyam tathā sati icchāmi abhayam api etad iti evam hi anyathā vadeta icchā viśeṣāḥ tābhyām ca jajñire anye sahasraśas  iti cetasi saṃdhāya yājñavalkyam apṛcchata iti cetasi saṃdhāya yājñavalkyaḥ abhyabhāṣata iti cetasi saṃdhāya sarva yoga īśvara īśvaraḥ iti doṣa apanatti artham yam na veda iti bhaṇyate iti dvayam pratīcī ā iva saṃbhāvyam brahmaṇi īritam iti pṛṣṭaḥ abravīgārgi mā atiprākṣīḥ katham cana iti prativacaḥ kaṣṭam matvā enam paryapṛcchata iti praśna prativacaḥ  yājñavalkyaḥ api avāca tam iti bhāllavi śruti vacaḥ samyak jñānasya janmane iti matvā athavā aprākṣīt pṛṣṭam artham panaṛṣima iti veda vid āpyaktam tad aprāmāṇya kāraṇam iti vyācakṣate kecid praśnau  etau yathā uditau iti vyācakṣate kecid agrantham etam mahā dhiyaḥ iti vyāsasmṛtau vākyam pratyakṣa śratibandhanam iti śrautam vacaḥ  jñeyam āgama eka pramāṇataḥ iti spaṣṭam śruteḥ vākyam kasmāt na ādriyate tvayā iti iti akta parām arśaḥ  hi atideśa artha ucyate itas anyatra ati mokṣā ye te api evam iti vīkṣyatām itas  muktasya rūpāṇi tu agni ādīni parābravam iti antaryāmi avasthāyām sthitvā ekām prāṇa devatām iti artham kopa kṛt vākyam śākalyaḥ  maniḥ abravīta iti arthe loka saṃsiddhām prasiddhim śrutiḥ abravīt  iti arthaḥ atra vidheyaḥ syāt anvaya vi atirekataḥ iti asya parihāra ukti kecid ācakṣate budhāḥ iti ācakṣata iti akti ānam ādoṣaḥ apanadyate ityādi parva pakṣa ukti daṣaṇeṣu abhidhāsyate ityādi parvam eva uktam dūṣaṇam dūṣita ātmanām ityādi su viruddham syāt na ca api iha aparā mitiḥ iti āha bhagavān vyāsaḥ sarvajñaḥ api mahāmatiḥ iti āhuḥ śrutayaḥ sarvāḥ smṛtayaḥ ca api anekaśas  iti akta parihāra artham na etad samyak iti īryate iti uktavantam pratyāha tad vakṣyāmi tava adhunā iti uktau  ati saṃvyāpti prasaktau  uttaram vacaḥ iti ukte tam ṛṣi bhūyas  sa pratiṣṭhām apṛchata iti uktaḥ ahallikā iti evam saṃbodhya uttaram abravīt iti ukti artha uparodhena vyācakṣīta parāyaṇam iti etad pratipatti artham tad vā etad iti śrutiḥ iti etad aviruddham syāt prasādāt jātavedasaḥ iti etad hṛdaye kṛtvā kāruṇyāt tam atha abravīt iti etad hṛdaye kṛtvā yājñavalkyaḥ  nirāha tam iti evam dharmakārāṇām api vākyāni koṭiśas  iti evam abhimānā yā na antaryāmī iti sā ucyate iti evamādi vākyāni yathā ukta artha samarthane iti eṣaḥ arthaḥ  vidheyaḥ atra yena iti vacasā śrataḥ idam tad tad idam ca iti triṣa kāleṣa nitya tāma idhyate aharniśam yasmāt indha nāmā tatas  pamāna indraḥ ca devatā jñeyā meghanāda abhimāninī indham santam tam ātmānam indra nāmnā pracakṣate indhaḥ nāma eṣa puruṣaḥ  dakṣiṇe akṣaṇi yaḥ sthitaḥ imam deśam yatas  prāptānādityāt yakta varmanā imām avasthām saṃprāpya sarvaḥ  brāhmaṇa ucyate imau dvau  eva panthānau karmata tyāga lakṣaṇau iyam tu na tathā sthūlā yām tvam pṛcchasi devatām iyatā yadi pāṇḍityam labhyate veda tarhi tam iyattā kāraka avasthā paricchid jñānam eva ta iyān eva ta deśaḥ ayam prāṇinām bhoga siddhi kṛta iva iti anarthakam kecid eva arthena virodhataḥ iha tu īśātirekeṇa na anyat kicid prakalpyate iha vā amutra vā jñānam jāyate mokṣa kṛt hṛvam īkṣyante ca api akṛpaṇāḥ tad ca sati eva yantari īdak eva phalam ca atra māna meya ādikam tathā īśitavya artha saṃbandhāt antaryāmi etad akṣaram ukta kārya atirekeṇa viṣadadhi ādivat mitiḥ ukta brāhmaṇa sādṛśyam sarva karma nirāsataḥ ukta vātirekeṇa na ātma vastu ghaṭa ādivat  yāḥ ukta akṣara ātmā vasitena kiṃcid avaśiṣyate ukta artha aparihāreṇa tad ajñān jabhamiṣa uktaḥ  niranvayaḥ abhāvaḥ  na bauddha ādi samāśrayāta ukta upāya atirekeṇa pṛcchayate sādhana antaram ukta upāsā phalam na atas  gantavyam vedmi kim cana ucitā dakṣiṇā eṣa eva yokta iha abhaya lakṣaṇā ucitaḥ asyāḥ  bhavet praśnaḥ  devatā yena pṛcchayate ucchinna kāma karmā asau kṛtsna tad phala bhogataḥ ucchinna aśeṣa baddhayā ādiḥ tad kāraṇa parikṣayāta ujjvalatva ādi sāmānyāt deva loka ādi saṃpadaḥ utkrāntau syāt anirmokṣaḥ  janma artham maraṇam yatas  utkrāmanti na ced prāṇā na ayam tarhi mṛtaḥ  bhavet  uttareṣu api vākyeṣu yathā uktam upapādayet  utpatti ādi prakārāṇām anityatva samanvayāta utpatti ādi phala udbhūtau muktiḥ astu tatas  phalam utpatti ādi viruddha tvāt mokṣa rūpasya nityataḥ utpatti ādeḥ anyatamaḥ  na ca mokṣa iha iṣyate utpatti ādi atirekeṇa saṃsāra vinivṛttaye utpatti ādi anvayāt tasmāt anityam syāt ghaṭa ādivat  utpatti ādi ātmakam kāryam sādhyam sarvasya karmaṇaḥ utpatti āpti vikārā hi saṃskāraḥ ca kriyā phalam utpanna samyak jñānasya saṃnyāsaḥ  lakṣaṇam yatas  utpanna ātma prabodhānām ātma avidyā tadat bhavam utsargasya asti viṣayaḥ  yaḥ anirjāta ātma tattvakaḥ utsarga apavāda vidhi niṣedhā ekala ātmani udāra phala dāyīni bahuśas anuṣṭhitāni api udīcī digadañcaḥ ca sarve sarvā diśaḥ tathā udgītha pramukhā ye arthā madhu kāṇḍe purā uditāḥ udgītha brāhmaṇe parvam aśvala brāhmaṇe tathā upacārāt kām iti tad asattvāt na karmaṇaḥ upadeśa śatena api brahma tvam na katham cana upadeśasya viṣayaḥ praśna pratyukti vākyayoḥ upanyāsaḥ  dvayoḥ atra vijñāna ātma para ātmanoḥ upapannaḥ tadā ārambhaḥ  mithas kārya pṛthaktvataḥ upamā artham iva iti etad padam atra prayajyate upavādinā iha viduṣaḥ  na bhāvyam kasyacid kvacid  upasīdanti tatra eva brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyān sadā upasthāpayataḥ karma tathā kṣapayataḥ  yatas  upātta sva viśeṣyāṇi sākṣāt iti ādikāni hi upādhibhatayā dṛṣṭayā hāna upādāna rūpayā upāsanam ca karma eva yaktam aktam idam tatas  upāsanānām sarveṣām aikātmya jñāna niṣṭhatā upāsanāni sarvāṇi para vidyā adhikārataḥ upāsanāni aśeṣāṇi tathā karmāṇi aśeṣatas  ubhayam tu iti atas  śeṣa advayam pṛṣṭam atas  bhaveta ubhe satya ānate tyaktvā yena tyajasi tam tyaja ulaka cakṣaṣaḥ arūpāt rasa ādi grahaṇam kvacita uṣasta praśna eva ayam kaholena api pṛcchayate uṣaḥ ta uktaḥ  viśeṣyaḥ atra kahola uktaḥ  viśeṣaṇam ūmrasaḥ  lohitasya atra piṇḍaḥ  yaḥ saḥ annam etayoḥ ūdhrvam divaḥ kapālāt yad adhas  yad ca adharāt paṭāta ṛddhi prāpat yatas  sarvam vāyau sati carācaram eka eva tatas  praśnaḥ  na praśna dvayam iṣyate ekam sat eka rūpam ca yadi nāma ukta lakṣaṇam ekaḥ sākṣātkṛta brahmā mṛterūdhrvam ca tad layaḥ eka kāraṇa sākṣitva kartṛ duḥkhitva rūpataḥ ekatra ca na saṃbhāvyau  ātmānau dvau śarīrake ekatra samavāyaḥ syāt samasta vyasta dharmayoḥ eka tvāt pavamānasya tadāhar iti codanā eka deśa upanyāsāt aikārthyam avasīyate eka deśānavasthānāt na samuccayatā tayoḥ ekadā ekatra na syātām prakāśa tamasī yathā ekavaḥ tu avasāyi tvāt anyonya artha anurodhataḥ eka vākya tvam etasmāt vaitādvaita artha vākyayoḥ eka saṃkhyā eva na anyā asti dvi saṃkhyāyāḥ  yatas tatas  ekasya eva hi devasya vibhāgaḥ sthāna bhedataḥ eka ātmakāḥ sarva dehā vivādaḥ  yeṣa vartate eka ādi dakṣiṇāsu etam vikalpaḥ tulya iṣyate eka artha tve api ca sati na eva asya punarukta tā eka artha praśna vākyasya hi ekā pratyaktiḥ iṣyate eka artha yogāt vākyasya na eka uktau syāvayā artha tā ekā lokaṣaṇa eva iyam tridhātaḥ vyapadiśyate eka āśraya tvataḥ sthāsnvī saṃsṛṣṭā iva upajāyate ekena eva kṛtārtha tvāt na anutiṣṭhet tatas aparam ekaikam makti kṛt cetsyāt yavati ihi ādi homavat  ekaikaśyena nītvā atha niṣṭhām pāṇḍityalakṣaṇām etam tam iti vākyena dṛṣṭi ādeḥ sākṣiṇam śrutiḥ etad tamaḥ abhisaṃbandhāt sākṣi tvam pratipadyate etad asya praśāstṛ tvam sva moha ābhāsa hetukam etad asya virodhi tvam kārya kāraṇa vastubhiḥ etad evaṃvidham sūtram āgama jñāḥ pracakṣate etad eva ta vijñāya vyat tiṣṭhanti eṣaṇā atrayāta etad evam anārtam syāt svatas siddhatva kāraṇāta etad vai tad iti prāha pratyak sākṣikam akṣarama etad moha samattha tvāt pramātṛ ādeḥ manāk api etam eva tam ātmānam viditvā uktena varmanā etam eva samaddiśya mantrī nārāyaṇaḥ tathā etasmāt eva niḥsṛtya śarīrāt sarvatas  gatāḥ etasmāt eva vijñeyaḥ  vākyāt na anya pramāṇataḥ etasmāt eva hetoḥ tām tarkaśāstreṣa tārkikā etasmin  akṣare gārgi sraji klṛpta phaṇi indravat etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsana vidhau sati etasyām samyak uktāyām na anuktam avaśiṣyate etābhiḥ iti atas yāvat śarīrāt iti codanā etāvat eva pratyakṣam sarva yāthātmya vedināma etāvat mātra yā athātmyam sarvasya jagataḥ tatas  etāvat mātra yāthātmyāt kārya kāraṇa vastunaḥ etāvat mātra yāthātmyāt kārya kāraṇa vastunaḥ enam bhatāni sarvāṇi iti apāsana phala abhidhā evam krameṇa niḥśeṣam jagat dhṛdhupa saṃhṛtam evam ca sati tad parṇam brahma kṛtsnam ca yajyate evam ca sati yāvatyaḥ  nāḍyaḥ  hṛdaya bandhanāḥ evam ced akṣaram tādṛkkatham asti iti gamyate evam ced brāhmaṇa uktiḥ syāt dhvasta avidya gṛhītaye evam ca eka tvam anayoḥ iha vyākhyeyam ādataiḥ evam tamasi api jñeyam kṣetrajñaḥ ca ātma saṃjñitaḥ evam tau saṃpradhārī etad akta doṣān abhiplatam evam dṛṣṭam yatas tasmāt gārgī papraccha liṅgataḥ evam dhvasta ātma mohasya kutas avidyā uttha vastabhiḥ evam parijihīrṣanti na ta nyāya uktiḥ īdaśī evam pārikṣitān sarvān agniḥ indraḥ  viyat pathā evaṃvid api sa śatruḥ upavādāt abhūt yatas  evam viruddha dharma tve na ca doṣaḥ asti kaś cana evam vṛndārakaḥ pūjya āḍhyaḥ  mānuṣa vittavān evam saṃsarataḥ tāvat param brahma parāyaṇam evam saṃsāra vidhvastiḥ tad hetoḥ jñāna hānitaḥ evam sati samarthaḥ syāt sarva āśrama samuccayaḥ yaḥ evam samāne saṃkṣepaḥ  vikāsaḥ ananta devatāḥ evam artham upoddhātam evam sa kṛtavān muniḥ evam eṣa samāna antaḥ śākalya praśna nirṇayaḥ eva arthasya upamām anya iva arthe ca avadhāraṇam eva iti avadhṛteḥ yad vā parva praśna artha śeṣa tā eṣa ātmā iti pratyuktiḥ yaḥ prāṇena iti ca aparā eṣa eva kramaḥ  jñeyaḥ prādhānya guṇa bhāvayoḥ eṣa eva ana saṃdheyaḥ  nyāyaḥ  yaḥ ayam iha uditaḥ eṣa eva ekalaḥ draṣṭā kāraka ādi vivarjitaḥ eṣaṇā kāma paryāyaḥ kāmaḥ ca aprāpta gocaraḥ prāpta gocaraḥ eṣa mārga upanyasta aikātmya jñāna janmane pākaḥ kṣiṇam eṣaḥ antaryāmi eṣa yoniḥ sarvasya prabhava apyayau aikakaऱyā dhruvam prāpat sarveṣām api karmaṇām aikātmya vaḥ tayā athātmyam abhipretyāta uttaraḥ aikātmya vasta vijñānam karmabhiḥ hi virudhyate aikātmyānavabodhasya kāryam aktam aśeṣatas  aikātmye vartamānasya brahma ātmā asya parāyaṇam aikātmye sarvam eva idam kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇam aikārthyam etayoāyyam mithas artha avasiteḥ tathā aikārthyāt praśna vākyasya na ātmānau dvau vivakṣitau aikārthyāt na iha saṃsargaḥ tad viruddha arthayoḥ iva otam protam ca tad kasmin  iti pṛṣṭaḥ  bravīhi me otam protam ca yatra idam tad akṣaram atha ucyate otaḥ protaḥ ca niḥśeṣa ākāśaḥ akāraṇa ātmani ota protaka tām vāyoḥ jagataḥ asau prayatnataḥ ota prota gira aśeṣa dṛśya vastu nirākṛteḥ ota prota ātma tām gārgī tayoḥ eva anvapṛcchata ota prota ātmanā kārya yena yena samāplatam ota protāni tattvāni tena parvāṇi sarvaśas  otāḥ protāḥ ca kasmin nu brahma lokā iti īryatām auṣaṇyam śaityam yathā atyeti vastu vṛttena sarvadā kaṃcid viśeṣam āpekṣya pṛṣṭaḥ  bhūyas api pṛcchayate katama iti pṛṣṭaḥ atha vasu ādīn pratyapadyata katamaḥ  yājñavalkya iti sa tam pratyāha śaddhadhīḥ katham evaṃvidham gārgi na asti iti akṣaram acyate kadamba paṣpavatsā eṣā devatā hṛdaya āśrayā kapāla saṃdhi gam vyoma sāmarthyāt parimāṇataḥ karaṇa ādi anapekṣasya na ca vijñāna saṃbhavaḥ karaṇa āyatanān devān sva pratiṣṭhān vrajet ta saḥ karaṇeṣu eṣa sarveṣa tathā kārya ātmakeṣa ca kartavyaḥ atas  vicāraḥ atra yukti mārgeṇa yatnatas  kartṛ kārya avabhāsi tvāt kartṛ kārya abhidhāyibhiḥ kartṛ tvam karaṇa tvam ca karma tvam ca ātma sākṣitaḥḥ kartṛ tvam ātmanaḥ  yuktam cit prādhānyāt ca bhoktṛtā ka ātmanaḥ purā siddheḥ buddhayādi vyatirekataḥ ka ādi ca ātma moha uttham vastu siddham svatas advayam ka ādi ca ātma moha uttham svatas akāraka tā ātmanaḥ kādeḥ iha sākṣi ātmā dṛṣṭeṣṭā ucyate adhunā karma kāṇḍāt apacchidya tena atra eva eṣa bhaṇyate karma kāṇḍe virodhi tvāt na eva enam vyācacakṣire karma kārya sajāti tvāt pāriśeṣya nayaḥ kutas  karma kārya antaram nityam viṣadadhi ādivat hṛvam karmaṇaḥ syāt praśaṃsā evam tad prādhānya upapattitaḥ karmaṇaḥ adṛṣṭa sāmarthyam yadi ajñāna apanunmatam karmaṇaḥ api tathā mānam na kiṃcid upapadyate karmaṇyāni bhavanti asya na ta tāni tathā yatas  karmaṇi eva ta vijñeyā nāsau  artha antare yatas  karmataḥ kālataḥ  mṛtyoḥ muktaḥ ayam svargam eṣyati karma darśayitavyam syāt daṣṭayā draṣṭā na dṛśyate karma prakaraṇe na ayam śrutaḥ parvam kadā cana karma pradhānāḥ paṃsaḥ syāt āśrayaḥ ayam anuttamaḥ karma prādhānyam eva atas  svayam eva abravīt śrutiḥ karmabhiḥ ca aviruddham yad devatā dravya tattva gam karma vyadhveṣu kurvanti yathāvastu ātma bodhanam karma vyadhva uparodhena hi anyathātvam prapadyate karma śabdena vidyā ca bhāvanā karma ca ucyate karma sidhyat yatas  dṛṣṭam pradhānam karma tena tad  karma atas kāraṇam makteḥ na katham cana yajyate karma atas teṣu sarveṣu pradhānam iti bhaṇyate karma ādi paratantra tvāt svāśrayaḥ  na ayam iṣyate karma adhikāra vicchedi jñānam ced abhyapeyate karma ārambhe vikaāva sva āśrayasya sadā iṣyate karma āśraya tvataḥ  liṅgāt avidvān iha gṛhyate karma itam karma tena idak vidyetam na katham cana karma īpsitatamam rūpam dṛṣṭeḥ kāryatva hetutaḥ kṣityāt eviyat antasya yāvana aikātmyam ucyate kṣiti ādau viyadante asmin sthūla ādeḥ saṃbhavaḥ  nanu kṣīyante anyāḥ ca bhogena cīyante anyāḥ ca karmaṇā kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin daṣṭe parāvare kṣetrajña parama ātmānau na atra ātmānau vivakṣitau kṣetrajña parama ātmānau na api praśne vivakṣitau kṣetrajña ātmānam aprākṣī t uṣaḥ taḥ  na param padam kṣetrajñeśvara saṃbheda śaṅkā anutyartham ucyate kṣoṇī upakramam ākāśāt ṣaṣṭhayantena abhidhīyate kṣmā kārya karaṇena eva kāryavān karaṇī ca yaḥ kṣmā ādi etad sūtra paryantam nāśāt arvam janeḥ purā gati gantavya gantra āderota prota ātma varmanā gatiḥ na viditā tasya tām sa tasmai vivakṣati gati vijñāna vaikalyāt paramātma vid api asau gati sādhanavat tvāt ca gantavyam anamīyate gati arthaḥ  na api ca praśnaḥ kva gamiṣyasi lakṣaṇaḥ gantavya ātmani katas  kriyā kāraka saṃbhavaḥ gantavyam pṛcchayate yasmāt na pipṛcchiṣitā gatiḥ gantavyam apamāna uktiḥ kriyate tasya sāṃpratam ganta gantavyayoḥ bhede virudhyeta na saṃśayaḥ gandharvam tatra kāle tam atha abrama kva te abhavan gandha ādi viṣayā dhī sthāḥ karma saṃbodhitā yatas  gamiṣyasi iti atas  vakti svāsthyam yātaḥ  yathā tathā gamyate lakṣaṇam tādṛṅana ca asau brahma vinmataḥ garta ādi atyayavattva tra na mānāt upapadyate gārgī akṣa rama nirdeśyam tām ca asau  abravīt idam gītayaḥ tu adhiyajñam tā adhyātma kā astu tā iti gaṇa bhāvam tadā yānti sarvāḥ tām prati devatāḥ gaṇān vā yadi veśānam kālam vā daivam eva vā garu tvāt lohavat pṛthvī dyauḥ api iti ati vismayaḥ gṛhāt ca pravrajet tadvat pravrajet ca vanāt tathā gṛha āśramam samāpya atha vānaprastham samāpayet  gṛhītvā paripapraccha śākalyam abhimāninam gṛhyate avidyayā abhinnaḥ maṇiḥ yadvat upāśrayaiḥ gautamena purā pṛṣṭe sūtrāntaryāmi vastunī grantha mayaḥ tu asaṃtrāsān na iha kṛtsnaḥ bhidhīyate granthe na anantare yasmāt ātma jñānam samīritam grahā ghrāṇāt ayaḥ  jñeyā gandha ādyāḥ tad atigrahāḥ graha atigraha bandhena tathā api sitam eva tad  graha atigraha rūpam tad prayaktam kena bandhanam graha atigraha rūpasya mṛtyoḥ karma iti niścitam graha atigraha rūpāṇām na atas  maktaḥ prajāpatiḥ graha atigraha rūpeṇa grastaḥ ayam iti kathyate grahaiḥ gandhādayaḥ  prastā grahāḥ ca ātmā ca gocaraiḥ grāhya grāhaka saṃbandhaḥ tad sākṣī na ca vīkṣyate grāhya tvam śaraṇam saṅgaḥ  bhayam ca ajñāna kāraṇam ghaṭa ākāśaḥ  mahā ākāśa iti akteḥ kevalam viyata ghaṭa ādi artha abhisaṃbandhaḥ  dharma adharma ādi kāraṇaḥ ghaṭa ādi ābhāsavat tasmāt na ātma ābhāsaḥ  vinaśvaraḥ cakṣara ādi grahāḥ tadvat prāṇa ādi sacivaiḥ iha cakṣuḥ manaḥ  vā buddhiḥ vā kartuḥ karaṇam iṣyate caturṇām katamena iti na tu praśnaḥ atra yujyate caturdhā pravibhajya enam sātvatāḥ paryupāsate candraḥ kartā iha tad prāptyā pakṣābhyām vipramucyate candreṇa manasā lokam avaṣṭambhena yāsyati caranti ūmra sa pūrṇāsu bhoga artham puruṣasya tu caritārtha tvataḥ amīṣām na apekṣā siddha vastanaḥ citi ātmā atra saparṇaḥ syāt āt iti ātmā athavā ucyate cit ajñāna eka hetu tvāt dhātavyānām cit ātmani cit ābhāsam svam ajñānam saṃnipatya tad akṣaram cit ābhāsa sva moha uttha kāryaiḥ tad vānivekṣyate cit ābhāsa eka mātreṇa tamaḥ siddhiḥ na mātṛtaḥ cīyam āna āditas  dehāt rasa ādi annena bhautikāt  cetanāvat svatantra tvāt devatā ātmatva kāraṇāt caitanya ābhāsa moha ākhya varmanā eva na tu svatas  jakṣat krīḍan ramamāṇa  ityādi śruti vākyataḥ jakṣat ityādi yad ca uktam tad ca api na virudhyate jagat ca api anabhivyaktam āvirbhavati sāṃpratama jagat jani sthiti dhvaṃsa hetar eṣa sadā īśvaraḥ jagat jani sthiti dhvasti niyama ādi artha kārī api jagataḥ ca api apādānam sva ātma avidyā samanvayāta jagat abrahma ātma saṃsiddhe taḥ maktiḥ kriyā udbhavā jagdhvā nitya ātmanā vidvān parṇa dṛṣṭyā avaśiṣyate jagdhvā mānena niḥśeṣam pratyakaparṇaḥ avaśiṣyate jaḍa tvāt iti parva uktaḥ  doṣaḥ atra api ca vidyate janakasya eva śiṣya tve grantha  chāyā upalakṣyate janitvā mriyate sarvaḥ  mṛtvā bhayaḥ ca jāyate janimat sarva bhūtānām prāṇe antar bhāva hetutaḥ janmanā eva āptam āpnoti svatas ameyam vacaḥ śravāta janyate yad phalam tādṛś kalpyatām nityakarmaṇaḥ jayaḥ  bhara ādi lokānām saṃkhyā āditva ādi sāmyataḥ jarā mṛtya tu dehasya dharmau  iti viniścayaḥ jarā mṛtya virājaḥ ca sarva kārya upasaṃhatiḥ jarā iti pariṇāmaḥ syāt valī palita lakṣaṇaḥ jale jalam yathā tasmin saṃsāri api ekatām gataḥ jalpe vādyatirekeṇa na anyaḥ  vakti yatas tatas  jāgrat deśa āptaye jñeyā nāḍī svapna ākhya bhamitaḥ jāḍyam janma ādi baddha tvam brahmaṇaḥ prāpnayāt adhravama jāḍya pāra arthya hetubhyām śaktiḥ na asti manāk api jāḍya anvayāt ca buddhayā ādeḥ yuktā tad kāraṇa anumā jāta eva iti atas asādhu yad uktam parva pakṣiṇā jāyate naśyati iti evam tad sākṣī api abhidhīyate jijñāsuḥ api ca etasya yathā uktasya ātma vastunaḥ jitvā deyā dvijān gāva iti artham ca uttarā śrutiḥ jihvemi atra punar vaktum punarukta girā bhṛśam jīva apetam iti hi uktejanma ādeḥ ca niṣedhataḥ jñātam brahma yathāvat ca na cāpāgāt tatas tamaḥ jñātayaḥ puruṣam pretam āhuḥ kāryam mṛteḥ idam jñātṛtva siddhaye jñānam jñātṛ tvam tad kṛtam yatas  jñātra ādi asaṃbhavam vakti kaṭa stha ekatva kāraṇāta jñānam muktvā tatas  prāptau na anyat kicid apekṣate jñānam hanti tamaḥ aśeṣam na tu karma tamaḥ nvayāt  jñānam hi vastu tantram syāt na tu tad kāraka āśritam jñāna karma phalam divyam yadi nāma para uditam jñāna kāryavat iti evam matam ced na evam iṣyate jñāna talyāmam anvānaḥ  dakṣiṇām gurave nṛpaḥ jñāna yuktam udīcyām ca karma evam upasaṃhṛtam jñāna yogena sāṃkhyānām karma yogena yoginām jñānavat jñāna saṃbhūte va prāk abhyupeyate jñāna svabhāvāt vayutthānam jñeyavaḥ tapa rodhataḥ jñānāt ca muktiḥ saṃsārāt katham na asti praśāstṛ tad  jñāna ajñāne tatas apekṣya vyavahāraḥ ayam ātmani jñānāt anyā gatiḥ ced syāt prāpsyasi iti eva tam vadet  jñāna anurūpām eva atas  dakṣiṇām ditsuḥ abravīt  jñāna anurodhinī yadvat pravṛttiḥ prāṇinām iha jñānena ajñāna vidhvasteḥ prātyakṣyāt tad asat vacaḥ jñāna utpattau kṣaye mānam karmaṇām vidyate yathā jñāna upabṛṃhitasya api kratu rājasya karmaṇaḥ jñeyatva siddhaye prāha yathā ukteśvara varmanā tam tvā pṛcchāmi śākalya tam mahyam brahi tattvataḥ tam tu aupaniṣadam devam sākṣāt ityādi lakṣaṇam tam tu aupaniṣadam dhīrā brahma ātmānam pracakṣate tam dṛṣṭi ādi dṛśam sākṣāt ātmānam kalpita ātmanām tam paṇḍitam iti prāhaḥ saḥ atra tyā niyajyate tam pratyāha amṛtam iti yājñavalkyaḥ api devatām tam prayāsyati kena ayam ākrameṇa iti pṛcchayate tam vāyum tad ca karma iha ya upetya vyavasthitaḥ tam samudram samuttīrya yad anyat paratas tatas  tathā eva na agrahīt su uktam śākalyaḥ kāla coditaḥ tathā eva yaḥ aśanāya iti paramātmā api śabditaḥ tathā eva vacasā uktiḥ syāt devaḥ  bhūtvā iti saṃbhavāt  tathā eva adhīta vedaḥ ca yuktaḥ sādhana saṃpadā tathā eva anya padārtheṣu tad vayoḥ api kāṇḍayoḥ tathā ukta tvāt purā na iha bhayaḥ  vaktavyam iṣyate tathā udarke pravakṣyāmaḥ sarvam bhadram tatas astu idam tad akāraṇataḥ kartum mṛtsnā ibhāśu ādikam yathā tad akriyā uktā śratyā iha tathā ātma jñāna janmane tad akṣaram pravaktavyam iti artha eṣa uttarā śrutiḥ tad atyaya ānaya antāni na santi pratyagātmani tad anuktau yatas  pūrvam sarvam syāt tuṣa kaṇḍanam tad antargatam ātmānam brahi antaryāmiṇam mama tad anya tvāt imām tu āhuḥ anati praśnyanāmikām tad anya bhāva asaṃsiddherāta tvam hetumat bhavet tad anya vyavadhāne hi pramāṇam na upapadyate tad anyasya tad ātma tvāt abrahmaṇi syāt katham gatiḥ tad anyeṣa padārtha īṣa pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇataḥ tad abhāve anabhivyaktam vastu na asti iti darvacaḥ tad abhyupagame vaḥ syāt anavasthā nivāraṇā tad ānanda ātmaka brahma vijñānāya manāk api tad āśaṅkā nivṛtti artham prārabdha eṣottarā śrutiḥ tad āhuḥ iti vispaṣṭam śrūyate śruti vākyataḥ tadat pattau sa saṃvid kaḥ mohaḥ  maḍha pradhānakaḥ tad utpatti ādimatsu eva yuktam kalpayitum phalam tad apādhiniyantā eṣa paraḥ proktaḥ  na ta svatas  tad eka deśa abhihiteḥ vijñāna ātmānam eṣyati tad etad loka nirmāṇa mota prota ātmanā uditam tad eva tad apekṣam syāt na tu deśa ādi siddhi dam tadā uta prota vākyena tad ca sarvam nirākṛtam tad ṛṣṭayā eva iha tam dṛṣṭvā brahma vadyam yadi īkṣase tad he tuhetumat tvasya prasiddhayartham atha avadat  tad ha idam iti ca atra api jagat eva abhidhīyate tad bhāva abhāvayoḥ ātmā na kāryam na api kāraṇam tadvat mṛtasya vaktavyam na tu putra prapautravat  tad vijñānasya nitya tvāt jānīyāt nityam eva tatas  tad vidaḥ tiṣṭhamānasya samāptiḥ syāt parāyaṇam tad vidaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ ca iha bheda hetoḥ asaṃbhavāta tad vināśe api tad sākṣyāt vinaśyanti iva lakṣyate tad viruddham katham paśyet ṛṣṭyā tad karma bhūtayā tad viruddham smṛteḥ vākyam na apekṣyam durbala tvataḥ tad viruddha ātmakaḥ pratyabrahmā parva ādi vākyataḥ tad viruddha ātma vijñānāt dhvaṃsitva ātmā ekalaḥ bhaveta tad na astitve api ca tathā tayoḥ tasmāt prasiddhitaḥ taniṣedha anavādena pratīci brahma bodhyate tad mala dhvastaye atha urvam paraḥ  granthaḥ avatāryate tad moha mātra je tasmāt eṣaṇe pratyagātmani tapasā kalmaṣam hanti vidyayā amṛtam aśnate tapaḥ  vidyā ca viprasya niḥśreyasa karam parama  tamaḥ prakāśavat karma na ajñānena virudhyate tam atyayam mokṣa vidhau tad vidvāṃsaḥ pracakṣate tamasaḥ  jñāna vidhvastau  abrahmān ātma tā āhateḥ tam etam iti ca tathā sarveṣām api karmaṇā āma tam etam iti vijñāya yathāvyākhyāta lakṣaṇam tam evaṃlakṣaṇam mahyam yathāvat vaktam arhasi tamaḥ  dhvāntam iti jñeyam atamaḥ akṣaram acyate tamaḥ mātra atirekeṇa vyavadhāna antaram na ca tamaḥ mātra abhijanataḥ na atas avidyām nihanti tatas  tamaḥ mātra eka hetaḥ ca moha saṃgatiḥ ātmanaḥ tayoḥ saṃcaratoḥ mārgaḥ  yā eṣoḥ vā hṛdayāt gatā tayoḥ samāgamaḥ ca asmina hṛī anta sthe saṣau mithas  tayoḥ aikātmyataḥ  yaktā na api tad nāśa iṣyate tava ātmā iti api nirṇītau na eva syāt praśna nirṇayaḥ tasmāt jñānam puraskṛtya saṃnyaset iha buddhimān devatāyāḥ  gatiḥ tasmāt vāyāyāniha ekalaḥ devatā liṅga karma ādi sarvam atra eva saṃśritam devatā avamペnā na aham gantavyam veśi kim cana devatā avāpti mātram hi tvattaḥ prākthatavān ahama devatā sama dāyasya bhedaḥ saṃkṣepa lakṣaṇaḥ devatā āsapa saṃhṛtya virājī api ca devatāḥ devatā sthāna karaṇa trayam prāṇagirā ucyate devatā asya striyaḥ  jñeyāḥ kāmaḥ strītaḥ  hi jāyate devatā upāsana ādi etad jñāna utpattyai vivakṣitam devayāji sakāśāt ca viśeṣaḥ ca ātma yājinaḥ deva loka ādi saṃpatsyāt dīpti mattva ādi saṃbhavāt deva saṃkhyām sa saṃpṛṣṭaḥ  nividā eva prapedivān devān apyeti saḥ agni ādīn śarīra tyāgataḥ param devāḥ  nividi yāvantaḥ  vaiśvadevasya saṃśritāḥ devāḥ ca pitaraḥ ca eva manuṣyāṇām adhīna tām devāḥ tu agni ādayaḥ  jñeyā vedāḥ ca eva prasiddhitaḥ deva upāsanataḥ pūrvam nābhat deva upāsakaḥ devaḥ  bhatvā iti jīvan saṃbhāvanā upacayāt naraḥ devaḥ  bhatvā iti devān hi pradhāna phala kīrtanam devaḥ  bhatvā iti vacasā tad kasmāt iha pṛcchayate deśa kāla nimitta ādi vyapekṣam vastu yad bhaveta deśa kāla ādi saṃbhedāt asādhāraṇa tattvayoḥ deśa kāla ādi aniyamāt pam icchānām ananta tā deha grahaṇa heta tvam yeṣām naḥ śrutiḥ abravīt  deha dvaya vimoke api na eva muktaḥ pumān iti dehaḥ tasya katham mṛtyarjīvasya iha upapadyate dehasya mṛtyu vicchedaḥ  viyogaḥ  deha liṅgayoḥ dehasya eva matena evam jīvaḥ  na mriyate sadā deha hadvāyavaḥ anyaḥ anya pratiṣṭhāḥ saṃhata tvataḥ dehāt asmāt paribhraṣṭaḥ karma prādhānya saṃśrayāta deha ādi nāśe tulye api tatra ekeṣām punarbhavaḥ deha adeha antaram gacchan kenacid pratihanyate deha ādi anātma dakta dvattatkriyām vīkṣate api na deha ādi ātyantikī hāniḥ anyeṣām yatra kāraṇe dehāntaḥ pratyak ātmā ayam pañcadhā gamyate miteḥ deha antara graha abhāvāt prāṇa utkrānteḥ asaṃbhavaḥ deha abhāvaḥ  hi mokṣaḥ ayam karaṇāni na santi atas  deha ārambhe na śaddhasya karmaṇaḥ śaktiḥ iṣyate deha indriya manaḥ buddhi dharmān eṣaḥ atyavartata deha indriya manaḥ baddhi prāṇādeniyatekṣyate deha indriya manaḥ buddhi vedanā vyatirekataḥ daiva vāc ādi saṃpattiḥ tathā vyanna ātma darśinaḥ daiva adhiṣṭhita eva ayam karma kāla vaśa anugaḥ dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ loke asmin  anyathā iyam samīkṣyate dravya dṛṣṭyā samīkṣyante dharmā nīlādayaḥ  yathā draṣṭavya ityādi vidhau pravarteta jaḍaḥ katham draṣṭuḥ anyasya ca abhāvāt na tam paśyanti devatāḥ draṣṭuḥ hi vyāpṛtiḥ dṛṣṭau dṛṣṭa rūpa ādi karmaṇi draṣṭa darśana dṛśyānām pratyak dṛṣṭi samīkṣaṇe draṣṭu darśana dṛśyānām saṃhatānām parasparam draṣṭṛ adarśana daśya artha prāptau  ādya viśeṣaṇāta draṣṭṛ adarśana dṛśya artha saṃbheda viṣayasya hi draṣṭṛ adarśana dṛśya artha saṃbhedasya niṣedhataḥ dvātriṃśa guṇitaḥ tāvān vyāptaḥ  bhāna gabhastibhiḥ dvātriṃśa gaṇitaḥ  mārgaḥ  ratha gatyā vivasvataḥ dvātriṃśadbhiḥ ahorātraiḥ yāvantam deśam uvrajan dvāram makham pratīkam vā yadi vā liṅgam acyate dvau  api etau mama ātmānau prāṇa eva pratiṣṭhitau dvitīyena ucyate tattvam pratyak moha nivṛttaye dvitīyaḥ  na iti yaḥ saḥ atha bhāvanā pratiṣedha kṛta dvaita t ṛṣṭayā eva niḥśeṣa dvaita kārya parikṣayāt dvaita bhedān imān sarvān ekaikasya na vetti yaḥ dvaita saṃsarga bādhena paṇa vastu pratīyate dvaitasya eti pum arthaḥ ca na atas anyat kicit iṣyate taḥ dvaitādvaita ātma saṃdṛṣṭayoḥ danta ula khalayoḥ iva dvaita arthasya viśuddhiḥ ca kīdṛśyatra vivakṣitā dhanam nisṛṣṭam rājñā iha brahmiṣṭha uddeśa taḥ yatas  dhana artham brāhmaṇā yānti rājānam iti yujyate dharmayoḥ samavāyaḥ syāt na tu nīlotpala ādivat  dharma adharma anapekṣa tvāt caitanya ābhāsa tām prati dharmī ca sarva dharmāṇām na parokṣaḥ tatas aśvavata vata dhāta na ta svatantram sanna avadat tejasi iti aṃtar  dhānāruhaḥ  yathā vṛkṣaḥ sākṣāt avyavadhānataḥ dhīḥ pāṇḍitya girā sākṣāt anvaya vi atirekataḥ dhruvāyām saṃhatiḥ nāmnaḥ  hṛdi evam sarva saṃhatiḥ dhvasta dhvāntasya vijñānāt atas  hetu phala ātmanām dhvasta ātma ajñāna tad kāryāḥ pratyagyāthātmya bodhataḥ dhvasta adhyātma ādi saṃbhedaḥ pratyak moha eka mātra bhāka dhvastā vidyasya ca aikātmyāt kaivalyena parāyaṇam dhvānta ucchittau vikartṛ tvam karmaṇaḥ tu anuvartate na kartṛ tā pramātṛ ādeḥ sākṣya tvena eva tad kṣayāt na karmaṇā kanīyaḥ tā vṛddhiḥ vā na antarātmanaḥ na karma tad phalam vetti na ca kasya eti saṃgatim na karma pūrva skandheṣa naṣṭa tvāt upapadyate na kaściniyataḥ  bhāvaḥ mṛtyar iti apadiśyate na kārakam na dhātu arthaḥ  na api yad syāt kriyā phalam na kārya karaṇam ca asya kiṃcid ātmīyam iṣyate na kiṃcid avaśiṣṭam syāt iti yadvat tathā iha tatas  na kiṃcid na jahāti iti prasiddheḥ idam acyate na ca karma phala tvena pāriśeṣyam prasidhyati na ca kambhāt iva dṛṣṭiḥ ātmanaḥ avyatirekataḥ na ca gaḥ dohana nyāyaḥ kāmya karmasu yujyate na ca tādṛś amṛtasya asti yasmāt tasya punarbhavaḥ na ca pramāda pāṭhaḥ ayam sarveṣām avigānataḥ na ca sattā iti sāmānyam pratyaya artha asam īkṣaṇāta na ca skandha atirekeṇa sthiraḥ kaścid api iṣyate na ca āgamasya svātantryam yukti ukteḥ apanudyate na ca ajñāna atirekeṇa vyavadhāna antaram matam na ca atyanta asataḥ janma karyāt loke api kāraṇam na ca anavasthā iha āpnoti sarva mṛtyatva kāraṇāt na ca anyatama eteṣām mokṣaḥ  yuktyā upapadyate na ca api kevalam karma paṃsaḥ syāt āśrayaḥ  yatas  na ca api tad abhāvaḥ ca na iti asthala ādi śāstrataḥ na ca api mithyā vijñānam paricchedakam iṣyate na ca api avidyā m asatī śaknataḥ kāma karmaṇī na ca ayam na iti na iti iti kāraṇa tvāt iha ucyate na ca avidyā atirekeṇa mukteḥ bandhaḥ anya iṣyate na ca aviśuddhe dvaita arthe śakyam advaitam īkṣitum na ca āśrama antaram yuktam mune[tthāyinaḥ sataḥ na ca aśrauṣam śruteḥ vākyāt karma mokṣa phalam kvacid  na ced jāmi bhavet vākyam pṛthak loka eṣaṇā grahāt  na ced te śaknutaḥ avidyām rakṣitum kāma karmaṇī na ced anubhava vyāptiḥ suṣaptasya abhyupeyate na ced āyatana ayuktam ekapād brahma tarhi tad  na ced vakṣyasi tam me tvam mardhā te vipatiṣyati na ca īpsitatama tvam syāt raṣṭrardaṣṭeḥ asaṃbhavāt na ca īśvare sthitiḥ tasya śāstra anārambha saktitaḥ na ca iha pariṇāmaḥ syāt attara skandha saṃgatau na ca iha laukikaḥ  jalpaḥ praṣṭu bhedaḥ  yatas  bhaveta na ca ekatra ekadā sthānam virodhāt janma nāśayoḥ na ca utpatti ādimat ki cid tatra sākṣāt phalam śrutam na jaḍam jñāna rūpa tvāt ānanda tvāt na niḥsakham na janya janakam vastu na dravya gaṇa karmabhiḥ na janyate atas  kṣīyeta na tu etad na iha janyate na jāne kva gamiṣyāmi katham vā iti abravī nṛpaḥ na jāyate janiṣyan vā tasmāt asti iha kaś cana na jñātaḥ kumbha vanā api cit stha tvāt khara śṛṅgavat na tatra dakṣiṇā yanti vidyayā eva tad ā āpyate na tad aśna ati vākyena yatas tad vāryate dvayama na tad ekatvataḥ  vetti brahma ānandam svakam tathā na tān prati samārambhaḥ siddha eva hi tān prati na ta deha grahe praśnaḥ sati gantari pṛcchayate na ta niḥśeṣa saṃsāra vidhvaṃsinī ātma bodhane na tu anāpadi vidyā artham tam yānti iha dvijottamāḥ na tu anyokti paritrāsāt yājñavalkyaḥ abravīt idama na tvayam mata iti asmāt kāraṇāt avasīyatām na tu ayoga vyavaccheda utkarṣaḥ tādagiṣyate na tu arciḥ ādivat tasya prāptaye gati kalpanā na dṛṣṭā niyatā ceṣṭā ratha ādeḥ jaḍa rūpiṇaḥ na deśa kāla avasthā ādau  apekṣā astyātmanaḥ svatas  na draṣṭrā uddeśyayaḥ pi tathā darśanayomithas  nana kriyāta eva iyam saṃsāra ucchittiḥ iṣyate nanu parvam ya uktaḥ arthaḥ sa eva iha api bhaṇyate nan brahma adhikāra tvāt katham ātmā iti anadyate nanu satsu api vākyeṣu na etad adhyavasīyate nanu sukhī aham asmi iti vijñānam anubhayate nanaktā madhukāṇḍe api dundubhi ādhupa pattayaḥ nanakta upaniṣadbhiḥ hi gantavyam prāc prabodhitam nanarmi ṣaṭaka atīta tvam daḥkhi tvam ca advaya ātmani nanu anaśiṣṭa eva ayam parva uktaiḥ anaśāsanaiḥ nanu eka tve vibhāgaḥ atra na asti kāraka saṃśrayaḥ na paśyeḥ pratyak ātmānam draṣṭāram dṛśyayā anayā na pāriśeṣya saṃsiddhiḥ tathā api iha upapadyate na bhatam tad pṛthivī ādi na api bhata gaṇāḥ tathā na bhata mātra upādāne bījam asti manāk api na mānam kiṃcid api asti jñāna karma samad citeḥ na mṛtasya iha retaḥ api vidyate kasyacid kvacid  na yuktaḥ ajñāna vidhvaṃsaḥ  balāt kalpayitum tvayā na ṛte dharām su vṛṣṭyā api padminī saṃbhavaḥ ambarāt  na ṛte liṅgam śarīrasya sthitiḥ kācid iha iṣyate na vā niṣedhaḥ sthala ādeḥ tasya prāk eva siddhitaḥ na vijajñau ca śākalyaḥ tam ātmānam yathā uditam na vyāvṛttam viśeṣebhyaḥ  na anuvṛttam ca gaḥ tvavat  na śarīram vinā liṅga kasmaicid karmaṇe kṣamam naṣṭe dvaite akhile na syāt samasta vyasta darśanam na sataḥ  vyatirekeṇa sataḥ anyaḥ  bhāva īkṣyate na saṃnyāsa vidhiḥ yasmāt śatau kṣatriya vaiśyayoḥ na samyak iti manvānā gārgya pṛcchat atas  punar  na samyak eta t vaya ākhyānam yathā tad abhidhīyate na sāmarthya yatas tasmāt na yuktā makti kalpanā na sāmānya viśeṣābhyām vāyoḥ anyasya vastunaḥ na sidhyet ā  ayoḥ uktam prayojanam idam dhruvam na sva kāraṇa saṃsargaḥ tasya jñānāt apahanateḥ na hi karma tamaḥ  hanti tamasi iva utthitam tamaḥ na hi pramāṇa virahāt asti vastu iti vīkṣyate na hi laukika cakṣubhi lakṣaṇyāt samarthyate na hi anyaḥ anya atirekeṇa saṃhatānām kvacid sthitiḥ na ākārakam samīkṣeta draṣṭu darśana gocarān na āgamāt aparam mānam maktau  abhyapagamyate nāḍīnām pariṇāhaḥ atha samyaktye ha varṇyate nāḍya ādhyātmikasya iva hi adhidaiva ātmanaḥ tathā nāḍī antareṣu api tathā sarvāsām saṃhata tvataḥ nāḍyaḥ ati sakṣmāḥ paṃsaḥ asya vyavahāra prasiddhaye na atas  saṃvedya ānandaḥ  brahmaṇi iha upapadyate na ati bhāraḥ asti naḥ baddheḥ śāstram ced tad param bhaveta na atas antaryāmiṇaḥ kalpyam anyat avyākṛtam badhaiḥ na atas anyat karmaṇaḥ kāryam na atas  maktau tad iṣyate na atas anyena pramāṇena praṣṭavyā devatā āgamāt na ātmanaḥ kāraṇāt anyaḥ kaścid saṃbhāvyate śruteḥ na ātma vidyā atirekeṇa pitarvaḥ tu antare yatas  na ātma ajñānāya sā yuktā sa hi sākṣāt tad īkṣate na ātmānam labhate karma yatas asaṃśritya sādhanam na ātmānam labhate karma yatas  vitta mate tatas  na ātma anātmīya kāryasya syāt apādāna kāraṇam na ātmā avidyām atikramya karma eka ātmyān arodhi hi na anayoḥ vyatirekaḥ asti bhokta bhogya ātmanoḥ kvacita nānātva ekatva rūpābhyām sā punar  prāṇa devatā nānat panna mitaḥ jñānāt kicid api avaśiṣyate na anekasya ātmanaḥ  nyāyyā tad asaṃbhava hetatas na antareṇa niyantāram tayoḥ eṣā vyavasthitiḥ na antareṇa niyantāram saṃbhāvya iti avasīyatāma na antavat abrahma rūpa tvāt iti vākya pramāṇataḥ na anyatra kṣatriyāt vidyā yatra saṃbhāvyate kvacid  na anya tra iha advitīya arthāt sākṣāt ātma artha saṃbhavaḥ na anyat ajñānataḥ astitvam dvitīyasya ātmanaḥ  yathā na anyaḥ anyāti viruddha artha vākyānām tatra darśanāt  na anvayam sahate pratyak na ca api vyatireka tām na api indriyam idam jñeyam yatas acakṣuṣkam akṣaram na āpnuyuḥ havya kavya artham yadi na abhat praśāsitā na api adhvastam tathā ajñānam kṛtsna jñeya samāptitaḥ na api anīśam apūrvam ca prakalpyam phala saṃgatau na api anvayam tad avyāpte pyabhāvaḥ satī iṣyate na api apūrvam kvacid daṣṭam tad māna asaṃbhavāt iha na abhau  niṣṭhaḥ anyatra api niṣedhaḥ kim ata akṣare nāma mātra avaśeṣam tad iti uktau gamyate yatas  nāma mātra avaśeṣaḥ asau  antarāle avatiṣṭhate nāma rūpa ādi sadbhāvaḥ  doṣaḥ ced iha codyate nāmnaḥ ca api upasaṃhāraḥ  dhruvāyām hṛdi varṇitaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ avyaktādaṇḍam avyakta saṃbhavam nārāyaṇāya viśvāya devānām paramātmane na avirodhāt tamaḥ  hanti karma kiṃcid kadā cana na āvediṣam suṣupte aham iti dhīḥ kiṃbalāt bhavet  na asti iti ta vinā mānam na sidhyet kambhavat svatas  na asya astitve yathā mānam eka tvāt akṣara ātmanaḥ na aham tad bhagavan veda yatra yāsyāmi atas  parama  na aham veda iti ca nṛpaḥ  jānan  api abravīt katham nityam bhaṅkte yathā eva annam ātmā vāc deha baddhibhiḥ nityam hi upaniṣatsu eva śrayate vaidikīṣu ayam nityakarma prasiddhayartham atas  vittam iha iṣyate nitya karma phala tvam ced makteḥ api abhyapeyate nitya karma phala tvena makteḥ api parigrahāta nitya karma abhisaṃbandhaḥ  makteḥ syāt pāriśeṣyataḥ nityasya karmaṇaḥ kārya pāriśeṣya samāśrayāt nityasya sarva karmabhyaḥ  vailakṣaṇyāt ca kāraṇāta nitya ātma dṛṣṭiḥ cit mātraḥ paśyet tam pṛthivī katham nityānām karmaṇām tasmin sati eva ghaṭate yatas  nityaḥ asya mahimā iti evam adarke api pravakṣyate nimitta tvena sat mānam sa ṣapta utthāpa koktivat  nimeṣa ādi vibhaktānām kāla aṃśānām vyavasthitiḥ niyacchati kṣitim devīm sarva avasthāsa sarvadā niyacchati yatas  gandhe trayam api etad īśvaraḥ niyatā eva pravṛttiḥ ca srotasām mahatām api niyantavya niyantṛtva saṃbandhasya prasiddhaye niyantā kāraṇam ca iti na ta satra antike asati niyantar api ced mā evam śruteḥ vastanī api dhruvam niyame hetu asadbhāvāt na syāt naiyamikī sthitiḥ niyamaḥ  yaktimān eṣa karmiṇām apapadyate niyamya devatā bheda vyāsa saṃkṣepa varmanā niradhāri purā tasya yāthātmyam tu atra pṛcchayate nirarthakam idam ca syāt daṣṭeḥ iti yad acyate niravidya advaya tvāt tad sākṣāt abrahma iti śabdyate niravidyaḥ asitaḥ  bhāsvat avilapta cit ātmakaḥ nirānandam tathā kecid kaivalyam pratijānate niruṇaddhi yathā janma tad nāśam api tad tathā niruhya kārya tām nītvā pratyahya atha ātma kāraṇe nireṣaṇa ātma saṃbodhāt bādhyaiva iyam atas  bhaveta   nireṣaṇa eka yāthātmye na yathāvastukāma dhīḥ nirgamayya aṇḍataḥ prādāt vāyave sakṣma rūpiṇe nitim āgamāt tasmāt pṛcchayate sādhana antaram niti viṣaya tvāt ca karma śakteḥ jagati api nirṇīta arthaḥ  na tāvat syāt praśnaḥ sākṣa ādi ti īritaḥ nirdeśyatva ānamā doṣa prasaṅga vinivṛttaye nirdvayam sa dvayam vā iti na ukta hetoḥ tad īkṣyate nidhūta aśeṣa duḥkha ogha hetu tvāt sukham eva tad  nirbījasya ca janma iha na āgamān na ca yuktitaḥ nirvidya ca tathā maunam padārtha dvaya saṃgatim nirvibhāga ātmanaḥ tasya prāñcaḥ prāṇāḥ purā asya ye nivartate sa kārpaṇyāt tad jñānāt dhvānta bādhataḥ nivartya tvena mokṣasya karmaṇā yad nivartyate nivivṛtsoḥ ta saṃsārāt maneḥ tyakta eṣaṇasya ca nivṛttiḥ kriyate yasya vidyatena iha karmaṇā nivṛttiḥ tadvat eva asya na avagatya ātmanaḥ aparā nivṛttaḥ  dvaita viṣaya ādi api eṣa tathā api tu niḥśeṣam brahma loka antam saṃhṛtya hṛdaya ātmanā niḥśeṣa karma saṃnyāsam vidyāyāḥ sādhanam śrutiḥ niḥśeṣa karma saṃnyāsam svayam eva pravakṣyati niḥśeṣa karma ujjhitim āha sākṣāta niḥśeṣa nirṇayokti icchaḥ kaholaḥ api āha parvavata niḥśeṣa paruṣa arthānām puṇyam karma hi sādhanam niḥśeṣam ātma saṃbodham karyāt iti vidhīyate niṣiddham akhilam vastu yad kicit jagati īkṣyate niṣedhati ātma vijñāne mantra varṇaḥ api kāṭhake niṣedhāya aparokṣā gīra bhinna artha grahāya tu niṣedhaḥ amukham iti evam trayasya api abhidhīyate niṣkalam tad param brahma na iti na iti apadiśyate niṣkriyaḥ cetanaḥ sākṣī sa kriyaḥ acetanaḥ parāṅ niṣpramāṇam yatas tasmāt pṛcchayate sa pramāṇakam niṣphalam ca bhavet jñānam yadi kāraṇa saṃgatiḥ nīlotpala ādivat nātaḥ saṃsargaḥ  brahmaṇi iṣyate nīhāra ādau tathā eva ātmā kārya kāraṇa vastuni na iti na iti iti yaḥ ca ukta iha upaniṣadaḥ pumān na iti na iti itivadvayā ākhyā sarva api iha samīkṣyatāma na iti na ityādi bhayāṃsi virudhyante vacāṃsi api na iti na ityādi vākyebhyaḥ  dṛṣṭi mātra ātma vastanaḥ na iti iti prathamaḥ śabdaḥ  marta amarta niṣedha kṛt  na iti iti vacasaḥ  vyākhyā tathā sati virudhyate na indriyāṇi asya vidyante na api tad svayam indriyam na iyam yakta aprasiddha īśe tad karma phala dāyini na īśvareṇa api nirvaktam samastavyasta tā ātmanaḥ na iha nānā iti vacanāt ekam eva iti ca uktitaḥ na iha atas bhaṇyate bhayaḥ anartha tvāt ca api anādaraḥ na aikātmyam śakyate draṣṭum klupta hetoḥ abādhayā na etad evam yatas  mokṣe vijñānam na upapadyate na etad yatas asaṅgam idam asaṅgaḥ  hi iti vakṣyati na evam karma tvasā ārūpyāt sā lakṣaṇyam bhavet na kim na evam nāma ādi saṃbhati piṇḍa prāṇa ādi saṃśraya na evam parihṛteḥ tasya mṛd dṛṣṭānta ādi yaktibhiḥ na evam yatas  pṛthivī eva śarīram yasya na aparam na evam yatas alohitam tad sarva rūpa ādi varjitam na evam yatas  na karmabhyaḥ  maktiḥ saṃbhāvyate aśruteḥ na evam vākyāt phalam yasmāt na kiṃcid api labhyate na eva atra gatiḥ asti iti spaṣṭam āgama śāsanam na eva anam invate trāsāt pṛthivī ādīn yathā tathā na eva upapadyate kṛtsna puruṣa artha avasānataḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ tad ajñāna mithyā adhībhrama hetatas  na eṣa doṣaḥ atirekeṇa na ātmanaḥ  brahma tā yatas  na eṣa doṣaḥ asti vijñānam syāt eva ānanda gocarama na eṣa doṣaḥ  yatas tatra yaktīnām apradhāna tā na eṣa doṣaḥ  yatas aprākṣīt yājñavalkyaḥ  narādhipam naiṣkarmya sādhanena eva brāhmaṇaḥ syāt yathā uditaḥ naiṣkarmya sādhaneṣu evam śrutayaḥ smṛtibhiḥ saha naḥ ced samasta dṛṣṭyā eva vyasta dṛṣṭiḥ samāpyate na utpādyaḥ  vā vikāryaḥ  vā vikāra pratiṣedhataḥ na upama iha yatas tāsām saukṣmye jagati vidyate nyāyaḥ sādhāraṇam sarvam viśeṣaḥ tu pravakṣyate nyāya akṣara anupātta tvāt yathā tad abhidhīyate nyāyyām vṛttim samat laṅghya tad viruddha tayā sthitiḥ pañcadhā iha upadiśyante tad etad anavarṇyate pañcama adhyāya śeṣeṇa paramātma vinirṇayaḥ pañcama ante vinirṇītam jalpa nyāyena sāṃpratama paṇḍitaḥ  na tu anevaṃvid yathā tvam paṇḍita āyase paṇḍa iti baddhi nām ā etad sā jātā yasya mānataḥ padārtha gatim evam vā vyācakṣīta avirodhataḥ pada āviṣayā ca iyam yuktiḥ tarkaḥ abhidhīyate padārtha adhigatiḥ parvam tatas tad abhisaṃgatiḥ padārtheka tvataḥ  bhedaḥ  dhvānta dhvastau nivartate papraccha yājñavalkyaḥ ata itas tvam kva gamiṣyasi para ārabhyate granthaḥ  brahma vidyā avabaddhaye paramātma svabhāvaḥ ayam svayam śrutyā prapañcitaḥ paramātmā eva gantavyaḥ paramātma vidā nan parama artham tu asaṃprāpya niṣedhaḥ  na iṣyate yatas  parama artha vidān na syareṣaṇā yā yathā uditāḥ parama artha ātma dṛṣṭyā iyam laukikī dṛṣṭiḥ ātmanaḥ parama udāra phala tā tu aśvamedha ākhya karmaṇaḥ para loka vināśaḥ api vidvat vidveṣa kāraṇāt paraspara ātta bhojyatva saṃskāra upanibandhanam paraspara uparodhena sva viruddha artha hānataḥ parāñci khāni iti tathā parāk pravaṇa sādhanam para ātmanaḥ paricchinnaḥ avidyayā uṣara rūpayā para ātmanaḥ svatas avidyā bahiṣṭhe kāma karmaṇī parāparatva bhedena dve vidye samudīrite parāyaṇam avaṣṭambha ātmanaḥ syāt tathāvidham parāyatta prabodhaḥ api śaktaḥ  vaktam yatas tatas  paricchinatti kim vyoma nīla jñānam manāk api paricchinnasya saṃvyāptiḥ vyākhyātā parvam eva tu paricchinna aparicchinnam tad ca karma svabhāvataḥ paricchetrī na ca avidyā tamaḥ rūpā hi sā yatas  paricchedam hi yad kāryam tad eva vinivartate pariccheda kṛt ajñānam sāsaṅgam mṛtya saṃjñitam parimāṇa mahā bhata prāṇa nāma anvaya ādayaḥ parimoṣiṇaḥ  yatas asthīni dhana śaṅkā pracoditāḥ pariśiṣṭasya kalpyasya sevye dṛṣṭatva kāraṇāta pariśiṣṭān api praśnānatkramya vyākara udasau parīkṣya lokān ityādi tathā ca ātharvaṇe vacaḥ parokṣa nāma grahaṇam tena devasya rocate parokṣa nāma grahaṇa priyā devāḥ  yatas tatas  parokṣa nāma grahaṇe prīyante devatā yatas  paryapṛccha yatha aśakti muktvā digjñāna mātrakam paryadāse api klṛptānām na pṛthaktvena saṃsthitiḥ pati lokam dvis tāvat pṛthivī pūrva mānataḥ paśa sādhana kaḥ  yasmāt yajñaḥ tasmāt paśaḥ smṛtaḥ paśanicchan kimāgāḥ tvam praśnān vā sakṣma nirṇayān pāṇḍityam atha nirvidya bālyam parisamāpayeta pāpasya karmaṇaḥ kāryam anyatra api mitam yatas  pārārthyāt sva artha virahe ṣaṣṭha gocaravat bhavet pārikṣitāḥ kva te abhavat nityuktiḥ tris iha uditā pārikṣita anatha ādāya vāyaḥ sva ātma samāśrayān pāriśeṣī naya dvārā mukteḥ karma phala ātma tā pāriśeṣī anayaḥ  na syāt sarvajñasya api anantatas pārthiva āpyau samāśritya tejaḥ abhivyajyate yatas  piṇḍa antar tāvat ātmā ekaḥ liṅga antaḥ tu tathā paraḥ pitṛ vrata uparodhaḥ atra na atas  kaś cana vidyate piṣṭa peṣaṇavat sarvam parva pakṣa ukti daṣaṇam paṃsaḥ karma kṣaye sva aṃśān saṃharanti yathāyatham puṃsaḥ deha grahe bhayaḥ  deha sthāneṣu devatāḥ puṃskāma viṣayāṇām tu na iyat teha upapadyate puṃsvabhāva anurodhena yuktiḥ vede abhidhīyate puṇyaḥ puṇyena bhavati pāpaḥ pāpena karmaṇā puṇya sādhana tā āśaṅkā mukteḥ api yatas tatas  paṇya apaṇya prayaktaḥ san graha atigraha bandhanaḥ putra eṣaṇātaḥ abhinna eva jñeyā vitta eṣaṇa ātmanaḥ putra utpattim samuddiśya dārān parijighṛkṣati panaruktam na ca nyāyyam eka pravacana sthayoḥ panaruktam na ca nyāyyam eka pravacane kvacita pum arthau  asiteḥ śāstram kṛtārtham vinivartate pumān janiṣyamāṇaḥ  vā saṃsārasya pravāhataḥ pamāśaya vaśāt ceyam phala klaptiḥ tvayā ucyate puruṣāḥ sarva eva amī punar dithupasaṃhṛtāḥ puruṣā na pravarteran na ced tebhyaḥ phalam bhavet  puruṣa artham samāpitsuḥ sa eṣa iti ca avadat  puruṣa arthatva sāmānyāt svarga ādi puruṣa arthavat puruṣa arthāya yad nālam labdha ātmā api kuṭhāravat  paruṣa arthe asati phale vidhānam na upapadyate puruṣeṇa iha janyante tasmāt sa puruṣaḥ akṣitiḥ paruṣe ye daśa prāṇā indriyāṇi saha ātmanā puruṣaḥ  vā iti hi uktyā tathā asmāt iti vākyataḥ purā uktā arthavatī ca evam sati sarvā bhavet havam puronuvākyāt yuktyā tu saṃkhyeya avinirṇayam pūrṇam tad akṣaram jñeyam sākṣāt ityādi lakṣaṇam parṇa ajñāna eka hetu tvāt rajju sādi dṛṣṭivat  parṇa ātmani tadā dṛṣṭe kaḥ kasmai kim praditsati parvam yadi viditvā iti tadā dvedhā prakalpanam pūrva karma upabhogaḥ  yaḥ puruṣāṇām śubha aśubhaḥ pūrvatra abhūt yathā sākṣāt iti pratyuktitaḥ  matiḥ parva diś ātma bhatam mām tvam viddhayā āditya devatam pūrva bhūmeḥ mucyamāna uttarām kām gamiṣyasi data parvavat ca uttaratra api sarvatra eva tridhā tridhā parva śakti nirāsena śakti antara samadbhavaḥ parvasmin pratiṣiddhe anyaḥ sāmarthyāt eva ḍhaukate parva uktasya eva dāḍhā artham praśnaḥ ayam pṛcchayate panaḥ parva uttara niṣedhyānām sāmarthyāt eva ca kramaḥ pūrva upalambha saṃskāra samuttha smṛti vibhramāt pṛcchantyā mardha pātaḥ te syāt eva sva aparādhataḥ pṛthivī devatā tarhi tvad akta artha samanvayāt pṛthivī yam na veda iti yad uktam tasya nirṇayaḥ pṛthivī anantaram sākṣāt samudraḥ śrūyate śrutau pathivī api ca yam devam na veda sva ātmani sthitam pṛthivī ādeḥ ca draṣṭu tvam tathā antaryāmiṇaḥ śrutam pṛthivī ādyāḥ tathā eva imā akṣarasya praśāsane pṛthivī āyatanam yasya tad sthaḥ agniḥ loke  eva ca pṛthivī eva aham iti evam yaḥ abhimānī vyavasthitaḥ pṛṣṭam bhūyas api ca apṛcchat ukta dhī dṛḍha niścitau pṛṣṭam yad yājñavalkyena na viduḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca yad  pṛṣṭaḥ adhyardha iti prāha sa upahāsam ṛṣiḥ sudhīḥ pauruṣeya vacaḥsu eva yakteḥ prādhānyam iṣyate paurvāparyam yathāyogam ktvā antayoḥ padayoḥ dvayoḥ prakṛtāyāḥ  vibhakteḥ ca vibhakti antara saṃśrayāt prajāpati tvam pitari tasmāt etad iha ucyate prajāpatiḥ virāj atra yaḥ aṇḍasya antar vyavasthitaḥ prajñā ādi upaniṣad kānyaḥ  dhyānāt devaḥ  bhavet iha prajñā iyam kim tatas  bhinnā pratiṣṭhā āyatane yathā praṇidhāya ātmani dṛṣṭi pratyak bodha eka rañjitām pratijñāta artha hāna āpte vam api apapadyate pratijñāya purā sākṣa āgām aham darśayāmi te prati deham vibhinnā ca tu asā dhāraṇa kāraṇāta pratiprāṇi ca vaicitrya ādeśa kāla ādi hetutaḥ pratibhāgam samāpta tvāt parva uktasya iha vastunaḥ prativakti eṣa iti tam yājñavalkyaḥ api udāra dhīḥ prativākyam bahu uktiḥ ca ṣaṇṇām ekatva siddhaye prativādi dhiyaḥ  yatnāt bhujyunā ākhyāyikā ucyate pratiśravaṇa velāyām śrotre yaḥ saṃnidhīyate pratīcaḥ asaṅga yāthātmyāt moha ādeḥ ca api avastutaḥ pratīcaḥ asti abhisaṃbandhaḥ  hi aśanāya ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ pratīcya ānanda viṣayam na pratyakṣam virodhyataḥ pratyak kaṭa stha rūpeṇa tathā sarva niṣedha kṛta pratyak kaivalya saṃsiddhau jñānāt eva tamaḥ hateḥ pratyakcit uparaktāyām buddhau dharma ādi hetukaḥ pratyak tattva parijñāna janma eva dhvaṃsa heta tāma pratyaktayā tad aikātmyam svayam eva pratīyatām pratyaktayā eva avasiteḥ pratīcaḥ anyasya vastanaḥ pratyakṣa nāma grahaṇam parihṛtya parokṣataḥ pratyakṣa nāma grahaṇam pradviṣanti jagati api pratyakṣam āviruddha tvam tathā ca ukteḥ prasajyate pratyakṣavat bodhayitum kim u pratyanirañjanam pratyakṣa śruti malaḥ ayam sarva āśrama samuccayaḥ pratyakṣa ādi ativarti tvāt yakti apekṣā na vidyate pratyakṣa arthasya eṣa iti na vidmaḥ kaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ pratyakṣa āsanna niṣṭha tvāt etad śabdasya kambhavata pratyakṣaka pramāṇaḥ arthaḥ  laukikaḥ api na śakyate pratyak saṃvitti vastu sthaḥ pramāṇa virahāt ayam pratyaksākṣī atirekeṇa na abhāvaḥ api prasidhyati pratyak ajñāna vidhvaṃse sāmarthya anityakarmaṇaḥ pratyak ajñāna saṃbhata kāma uttham sādhana ātmakam pratyagaikātmya saṃbodhāt tad dhamaiḥ lakṣyate katham pratyak jñāna samutpattau viniyogaḥ pradarśitaḥ pratyak jñānasya na eva atas  karmaṇā syāt samaccayaḥ pratyak jñāna udaye atas  syānivṛttiḥ sarva karmaṇām pratyak dhvā antam cit ābhāsam sva kārya niyama ātmakam pratyak bodha eka yāthātmya vasta mātra uparodhataḥ parodhataḥ pratyagyāthātmya dṛṣṭi ātmā kāraṇam sva tamaḥ vadhi pratyagyāthātmya mohasya kāryeyat ta iha bhaṇyate pratyagyāthātmya mohasya mahimā eṣa tvayā uditaḥ pratyagyāthātmya vijñānam na bādhyam bādhakam yatas  pratyagyāthātmya vijñānam na anavasthāpyataḥ  bhavet  pratyagyāthātmya vijñānam mṛtyarajñāna rūpiṇaḥ pratyagyāthātmya vijñāna sādhanatva prasiddhaye pratyagyāthātmya vijñāna svabhāvaḥ ced samarthyate pratyagyāthātmya vijñānāt tad tamaḥ  na ātma bādhataḥ pratyagyāthātmya saṃmohaḥ kriyā kāraka rūpavān pratyagrapa avabodhasya bhāva abhāva ātmavaḥ taṣa pratyagvastaparodhena nānā arthaḥ  na avaśiṣyate pratyak vastu atirekeṇa na anyat ātmā tadā īkṣyate pratyak virodhataḥ tadvat na kiṃcid na api nihnatam pratyaṅabhihitaḥ  yatnāt tad girā saḥ atra yujyate pratyak mātra tayā eva atas anātma ātmani vilīyate pratyak mātra svabhāva tvāt brahmaṇaḥ avyavadhāna tā pratyak mātrau  aśeṣa tvāt katas  ṣaṣṭhī artha saṃbhavaḥ pratyaṅa mātra avaśeṣa tvāt syām apūrva ādimān aham pratyak mātra ekayāthātmyāt ātmā avidyā tadatthayoḥ pratyaṅa moha ja baddhayā ādi jaḍa rūpa pradhānataḥ pratyak mohasya na atas  syāt jñāna karma samaccayaḥ pratyarthini śruteḥ vākye satya aikātmya avabodhini pratyavāya ādi bhāvaḥ ca phalam nityasya karmaṇaḥ pratyāyya evam para ātmānam maniḥ āha narādhipam pratyāha eṣa ta ātmā iti yājñavalkyaḥ api pūrvavat  pratyuktiḥ gārgi vāyau  iti evam eva uttareṣu api pratyuktiḥ ca tava ātmā iti bhinna arthe vacasī katham pratyukteḥ eṣa ta iti praśnayoḥ ubhayoḥ api pratyuccārya atha gārya uktam ākāśe prābravīt ṛṣiḥ prathate aneka rūpa ābham tad jñānam jñātṛ kartṛkam prathate apāsta niḥśeṣa kriyā kāraka vastani pradhāna guṇa bhāvena sarvatra ete vyavasthite pradhvasya ātmā ayamatyeti tad attham vasta vṛttatas pramāṇa jñāḥ praśaṃsanti yad ca tad ca sati īśvare pramāṇa balataḥ prāptam api bhari na vāryate pramāṇa bhamau sthitvā etad uktam sarvam prasidhyati pramāṇa varmanāyātam idam moha apanattaye pramāṇa vyāpateḥ tarvam vāsanā dhāna kāraṇāta pramāṇasya ca tad sarvam akṣare pratiṣidhyate pramāṇa avagateḥ tatra kim cintyam iti ced matam pramāṇa asaṃbhavāt tasmāt asamīcīnam ucyate pramāṇa asaṃbhavāt mā evam vocaḥ  laukika vastavat  pramātṛ dṛṣṭiḥ ekā atra śabda ādi artha avalehinī pramātṛ pariṇāma tvāt pramā siddhiḥ pramātari pramātṛ atiśayena eva kāraṇam syāt pramātṛ api pramātṛ vyavadhānena saṃvid ā eva na vṛttibhiḥ pramātṛ ādi padārthaḥ tu dharma adharma ādi hetukaḥ pramātṛ ādi pravṛtteḥ prāc sadāna stamita uditā pramātṛ ādi vyapekṣeyam laukikī dṛṣṭiḥ ātmanaḥ pramātrādi atirekaḥ api vastunaḥ  bodha rūpiṇaḥ pramātṛ ādi abhisaṃbandhaḥ  yathā anubhava siddhikaḥ prayuktāḥ karmaṇā puṃsām vartante bhoga siddhaye prayañjate hi ghrāṇādon  tatas te si arati grahāḥ prayoga rūpeṇa eva atas  veṣṭitam karma tiṣṭhati prayoga samavāyi eva dravyaka disādhanam prayogau  asiteḥ tarvam kālaḥ prāk ca prayogataḥ prayoge dakṣiṇāyām ca samānaḥ ayam parikramaḥ prayojaka ādi niḥśeṣam mriyamāṇā dvipaścitaḥ prayojaka avadhṛtaye yājñavalkya iti avāca ha prayojyasya hi bandhasya prayojakam iha uditam pravaktā yājñavalkyaḥ atra tam pṛcchanti aśvala ādayaḥ pravaktum upacakrāma putra vitta eṣaṇā eka tām pravartatām ced paruṣaḥ  na evam api apapadyate pravartate purā ivātaḥ brahmaṇi apyaya siddhaye pravāha rūpī saṃsāraḥ  dīpa arciḥvat avasthitaḥ praviviktatara āhāram śrutiḥ sūkṣma anna saṃsthiteḥ praviviktatara āhāraḥ  liṅga ātmā ayam purā uditāt  praviviktataraḥ anna aṃśaḥ tarpayan prāṇa devatāḥ praviṣṭasya na ced kātsnyam vijñāna ātmana iṣyate pravattā ākhyāyikā sā iyam samāptān avaśeṣataḥ pravṛttiḥ apravṛttiḥ vā devatā aiśvaryataḥ sadā pravṛttiḥ arateḥ kāryam mohasya anartha saṃplatiḥ pravṛttiḥ yena tena ebhyaḥ  jña ātmānyaḥ abhyapagamya tāma pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ  yogaḥ  jñānam saṃnyāsa lakṣaṇam pravrajet ca param sthānam pārivrājyam anttamam praśāsana idam tasthau yasya antaryāmi rūpiṇaḥ praśāsana mate śāstana vyavasthedaśī bhaveta praśāsane yathā rājñaḥ abhinna marya ādikāḥ prajāḥ praśnam yad idam iti evam yājñavalkyam mahā dhiyam praśna prativacaḥ tena brāhmaṇaḥ syāt yathā uditaḥ praśna śeṣam atha idānīm svayam eva śrutiḥ jagau praśnasya viṣaya tvena vijñāna ātmā upayogataḥ praśna arthā prathama uktiḥ syāt pratyukti arthā tathā parā praśnena bhāvitaḥ taṣṭaḥ pāṇim asya agrahī daṣiḥ praśnaḥ ayam na tṛtīyaḥ syāt pratijñāta tvataḥ  dvayoḥ praśnaḥ ayam sādhana jñaptyai brāhmaṇasya iha pṛcchayate praśna uktiḥ eka rūpā ca pratyabhijñāyate añjasā praṣṭum na eva adhikāraḥ atas abrahmiṣṭhasya iha vidyate praṣṭra bhedāt adoṣaḥ ced mā evam pratyakti bhedataḥ prasajya paryadāsābhyām nañarthaḥ kaḥ atra gṛhyate prasiddhiḥ iti tām āha tasmāt iti evamādinā prasūti mātrāt eva asyā dhvastiḥ ātyantikī bhavet  prāktanāni api janmāni samyak jñānam tu hanti naḥ prāc pramātṛ ādi saṃbhateḥ yad pramātra ādi kāraṇam prāc phala udbhavataḥ  naṣṭvā pratīci vyavatiṣṭhate prāk api brahma vijñānāt siddham tādātmyam ucyate prāk api brahma vijñānāt abrahma eva ābhat yathā tathā prāk api aikātmya vijñānāt avicārita siddhikā prāk eva asmābhiḥ uktaḥ asau yathāvat apapattibhiḥ prācī diś eva saṃvattāḥ tad avaccheda hānataḥ prācyām kiṃdevataḥ asi iti vidagdhaḥ tam apṛcchata prācyām rūpa upasaṃhāraḥ  diś traye karma saṃhatiḥ prāṇam brahma tyaditi āhar  pārokṣyeṇa mahā dhiyaḥ prāṇana ādi anumānena grāhayitvā dhiyaḥ param prāṇa mātra vināśe syāt bhūyas  janma prayojakāt  prāṇa śabdena ca api atra kāraṇa ātmā abhidhīyate prāṇa svān tatana dharmā aśanāya ādi lakṣaṇāḥ prāṇā eva vilīyante kim vā anyat api kṛtsnataḥ prāṇāḥ sa hetavaḥ sarve tadā eva āstā niranvayāḥ prāṇa ātma tvāt ca buddhayā ādeḥ piṇḍa antasya api anātma tā prāṇa ātmā eka eva āste prajñāna ghana vigrahaḥ prāṇa ādi kārya karaṇaiḥ svatas asaṃhata ekalaḥ prāṇa ādeḥ pratyak ātmānam babodhayiṣa rañjasā prāṇa adhikaraṇe pūrve śoka mohau manogatau prāṇa apāna vyāna rūpā adhyātma tāḥ pracakṣate prāṇena prāṇiti iti uktaḥ  dṛṣṭeṣṭa iti coditaḥ prāṇaḥ apāne sa ca vyāna udāne vyāna āśritaḥ prāṇaḥ ayam aniruktaḥ  hi kaḥ tam nirvaktam arhati prāṇaḥ  devaḥ ata eva ekaḥ tasya eva mahimā paraḥ prādhānyam yājñavalkīye yuktīnām abhidhīyate prādhānyena iha karma eva tad anyat tapa sarjanam prāpta aśeṣapamarthaḥ ca brāhmaṇaḥ atra abhidhīyate prāptaḥ asi iti ca nirdeśāt jñānam eva ātmanaḥ  gatiḥ prāptaḥ asi iti muneḥ ukteḥ parihāraḥ  na yujyate prāptaḥ asi iti yatas  jñāna janma mātram pravakṣyati prāptaḥ asi abhayam iti evam bhaya heta vināśataḥ prāpnoti liṅgam āhāraḥ sa tasya iti abhidhīyate prāmāṇyasya purā ukta tvāt tad siddheḥ ca anumānataḥ prāvartanta tatas  bhītāḥ karmasu ajñāta tattvakāḥ prāha asya vidyamānasya vikriyā mātram eva ta prāha imam eva bahaśas  prāṇinām hita kāmyayā pretībhataḥ asi nanam tvam pretavat bhāṣase yatas  pretya saṃjñā iha na asti iti atireva niṣedhati phalam katham na na bhavet viśvajit nyāya īryatām phalam ca jñāna yaktānām karmaṇām etad iṣyate phalam rūpa upalabdhiḥ ca kartar dṛṣṭi avasān jam phala dātṛtva sāmarthya dānam ca abhyadhikam tathā phalavat karmaṇām kvāpi kiṃcid sāmānya saṃśrayāt  phala saṃpada eva etā na atra karma vivakṣyate phala āpti kalpanā siddhau  apanyāyaḥ anyathā bhaveta phala abhisaṃdhi rahitam vidyetam karma maktaye phala artha īṣaṇayā ekatva prasiddhayartham atas  śrutiḥ phalena asya abhisaṃbandhāt niṣkāmam nityam ucyate bandha hetu api mokṣāya viruddha phala kṛt yathā bahis gatāsu nāḍīṣu viṣaktā hṛdayāt adhi bahu draṣṭu niṣedha artham na anyaditi āyudīraṇam bādhitva ajñāna saṃsārau yāti apūrva ādi rūpa tām bādhya eva ātma saṃmohaḥ  na tu asau bādhakaḥ  yatas  bādhya bādhaka bhāvāt ca pañca asya uraṇayoḥ iva bādhya bādhaka bhāvena kāmam astu samuccitiḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ ayam na tayoḥ yajyate tatas  bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ ayam virodhāt haṭate tayoḥ bādhya bādhaka rūpam ca na vyati iti prakāśayana bālyam ca eva yathāyogam anvaya vyatirekataḥ bālya śabda abhidheyā syāt tām samāpayya śuddha dhīḥ bāhya meya pradhāna tve satya sādhāraṇa artha dhīḥ bījam kāryasya sarvasya prājñaḥ ca iti nirucyate bījāt vanaspateḥ janma malāt ca iha upalabhyate baddhayā ādibhiḥ tathā ātmānam bhrāntaḥ adhyāropya ceṣṭate buddhayā ādeḥ abhisaṃbandhaḥ  janmanā eva cit ātmanā baddhayā ādeḥ pravilīnatva ai ha ādeḥ ca jaḍa tvataḥ baddhayantā dvayatiriktaḥ asti sākṣī praśnasya gocaraḥ baddhayantaḥ para eva ātmā vijñāna ātmā iti bhaṇyate baddha yāgama apāya sākṣī niyantā eva ucyate paraḥ buddhi tad vṛtti sākṣi tvāt buddhi tad pratyayaiḥ ajaḥ buddhi sākṣī tṛtīyaḥ syāt yaḥ ayam saṃdihyate tathā babhakṣa ādi niṣedhaḥ ayam tathā api ātmana ucyate babhakṣa ādi eka deha stha niṣedhāt aniṣedhataḥ bṛhat vicāre samyak ca prāk api etad vicāritam bṛhaspati save yad vakṣatriyaḥ  na pravartate brahmacaryam samāpayya gṛhī tasmāt bhavet advijaḥ brahmacarya āśramāt eva pravrajet iti bhariśaḥ brahmacarya āśramāt eva yadi vā pravrajet advijaḥ brahmaṇaḥ api ātmanaḥ  mohāt abrahma tvam na vaḥ tatas  brahmaṇaḥ  vā upadeśaḥ syāt athavā abrahmaṇaḥ  bhaveta brahmaṇi avasthitasya api tu akṣaya tvam śratiḥ jagau brahmaṇi ānandaḥ saṃvedyaḥ  laukika ānandavat yadi brahmaṇi ānanda śabdaḥ ayam prayaktaḥ sakhavācakaḥ brahma tvam anyaḥ  veda iti tadā ekatvam virudhyate brahma tvasya svatas  siddhebrahmaṇi syāt anarthakaḥ brahma vā idam iti ukteḥ prāk api jñāna janmataḥ brahma vā idam iti evam tathā brahmā eva san  iti brahma vid tve tu rājñaḥ asya mitim na upalabhāmahe brahma viddhi tad eva tvam na tu tad yad apāsate brahma viddhi tad eva tvam na tu idam yad apāsate brahma vidyā kimartheyam na anyat makteḥ phalam tatas  brahma vidyā adhikāra tvāt iti etad adhana ucyate brahma ākāśaḥ pratiṣṭhā ca nāma upaniṣad acyate brahma ākāśaḥ pratiṣṭhā syāt prajñā asya upaniṣad tathā brahma ajñānam yatas  hetareṣaṇānām na vastutas  brahmāṇḍa saṃpaṭaḥ tasmāt pareṇa abhyeti sarvatas  brahmāṇḍāt vahiḥ antar ca samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi rūpiṇaḥ brahma ātmani samāpta tvāt gatiḥ kā parama ātmani brahma ātmanoḥ asaṃsargaḥ tad viruddha arthayoḥ iva brahma ātmā eka svabhāvena sākṣāt iti viśeṣyate brahma ādīni ca bhūtāni grathitāni akṣa sūtravat brahma ānandam atha anyaḥ san veda maktaḥ  ghaṭa ādivat  brahmā viśvasṛjaḥ vākyāt deva sāṣṭarī atirekataḥ brahma iha paramātmā uktaḥ  lokā bhara ādayaḥ tathā brahmā eva ced avidyāyāḥ  janmanaḥ kāraṇam matam brahmā eva brāhmaṇaḥ sākṣāt apacārāt parāyaṇam brahmā eva san  ava āpnoti brahma iti vacanam sphaṭam brāhmaṇa tvānahamānī vipraḥ  vā kṣatrakarmaṇi brāhmaṇānām atas  yaktam phala paryavasāyinām brāhmaṇāḥ tad vadanti iti sva aparādha niṣedha gīḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ ghātayiṣyāmi mām jighāṃsantam āśvimama brāhmaṇyam gauṇam anyatra pūrva bhamiṣu na añjasā bratātas  jagataḥ  malam yatas  bhayaḥ abhijāyate bhagavan  anuśādhi iti yathā iha abhimatam tava bhaya hetuḥ avidyā eva sā ca duḥsthita siddhikā bharaṇāt sarva kāryāṇām prāṇaḥ  brahma iti bhaṇyate bhavān api aham eva iti yadā sākṣāt viniścayaḥ bhaviṣyat ca yadāgāmi na atītam na api vartate bhaviṣyat loka saṃbandhī yeṣām āgamataḥ  mataḥ bhāna prakāśa saṃvyāptaḥ  virājaḥ  vistṛtiḥ tu iyam bhāna prakāśa saṃbandhe bhānoḥ na anyat apekṣate bhāna syandana gatyā adhvā mitaḥ  yāvān aharniśam bhāvanā gocaram jñānam bāhya vastu avalambanam bhāvanā ādi viśeṣeṣa yad śānteṣu avaśiṣyate bhāvanā upacayāt devaḥ  bhatvā vidvān iha eva ta bhāva abhāva dvaya dhvaṃsi brahma vedyam ca tad vidaḥ bhāva abhāva atireki tvāt abhyapetam tvayā ucyate bhāva abhāvau na vastveti pratyākhyātam yadātmanā bhāṣya upāttamatas  bramaḥ  na anupāttam katham cana bhikṣayā lakṣyate caryā hi ākiṃcanya eka saṃśrayā bhikṣā caryam caranti iti vidhi arthaḥ kriyate mahāna bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ bhinna māna pramātra ādau kārya kāraṇa vastani bhatam yad samatikrāntam bhavat yad adhunātanam bhata mātrāḥ pradīpasya saṃtānena āciṣaḥ  yathā bhatāni kṣīyamāṇāni karmaṇā paramātmanaḥ bhatāni ca eva sarvāṇi vāyanā prathitā ani atas  bhatāpi itim manaḥ sākṣāt arśayati avinaśvarīma bhamā tad sakham iti evam chāndogya upaniṣad vacaḥ bhayaḥ api iha pravakṣyāmaḥ prasaṅga ana ati vistarāt bhayaḥ aprākṣīt muni vidvān yāthātmya arthau  abuddhaye bhari kāraka sādhyā ca kriyā loke api dṛśyate bhūri dūṣaṇam atra uktam śrutyā ca svayam eva ca bhari sādhana sāpekṣā sukha daḥkha phala pradā bheda saṃsarga hīnaḥ arthaḥ sva mahimni vyavasthitaḥ bheda saṃsarga hīnaḥ arthaḥ tad hetadhvaṃsa varmanā bheda hetṛ ta maḥ gha ati pratyagyāthātmya śemaṣī bhoktari iha yadābhāti tad pramāṇa phalam smṛtam bhoga kṣayeṇa kāmyānām niṣiddhānām ca karmaṇā āma bhoga mokṣa abhisaṃbandhī yam pratyetat pravartate bhogya tvāt sā virāj uktā taga uktā dakṣiṇa akṣi gaḥ bhraṇa hatyā aśvamedhābhyām na param pāpa paṇyayoḥ matam ced na phala tvena mokṣaḥ  nityaḥ abhyupeyate matam jakṣaṇavat muktau sarva ātmatva atyara ātmanaḥ matam na jāyamānaḥ asti jāta tvāt eva kāraṇāt  matam ajñānam eva etad karma nāśayati iti ced  mattaḥ śarīrāt kvā anyatra mayi eva atas  pratiṣṭhitam madhye vākya  chidaḥ abhāvāditi śabdasya pūrvavat  manaḥ ca jyotiḥ vijñānam saṃkalpa ādi sva lakṣaṇam manasā manate yad na yena ca aharmanaḥ  matam manasā ekādaśa atra etān udān ityācacakṣire manasaḥ agrahaṇam tasya na dṛṣṭeḥ iti vāraṇāt  mananā api ātmayāji iti yad aktam para darśane manaḥ adhiyajñam brahmā eva brahmā candraḥ adhidaivatam manaḥ adhyātmam yad asya abhada brahmā ca eva adhiyajña gaḥ manḍalīkarate bhānaḥ tāvān  loka rava īritaḥ mantra āmnāyaḥ api apanyastaḥ  yathā iha na virudhyate mantraḥ api ca aikātmya viniścayāya mama ātmanām anekeṣām saṃbhavāt aprabodhataḥ mama iva bhavataḥ apodam na ca kiṃcid asaṃgatam mayā ayamana yātavyaḥ kartā ca ayam mama abhavat  mayi agnau śiśavat mohāt praviśantam na kaśa cana martyaḥ svid matyanā vṛkṇaḥ kasmāt malāt prarohati martya janma tathā sākṣāt yatas tad abhidhīyatāma martyasya janma m alam yad tad brata brāhmaṇā mama mācśata guṇena ata uttara uttara vṛddhitaḥ mahimā viṣkṛtaḥ śrutyā vidyā yuktasya saṃbhramāt  mahyam prativacaḥ  vācyam doṣaḥ tu syāt tatas anyathā mām pratyevaiti iha yathā sādhāraṇyena bhāskaram māgocara ati varti tvādat aṣṭam syāt tad akṣaram māgocara ati varti tvāt asā dhāraṇa dṛṣṭitaḥ mā jñāsiṣṭa katham nāma nāma tattvam bahis janaḥ māṇḍakeya śrati vaca iti spaṣṭam adhīyate mātā mātari mānam ca mānāt meyam prasidhyati mā atītya praśna viṣayam gārgi prākṣīḥ katham cana mātṛ
